- **Verifier:** removeYear (RatesEditor.tsx:354) and removeCurrency (line 374) unconditionally setDirty(false) after persisting only their own cleared cells, while Save is gated disabled={!dirty} (line 827) and cell edits persist ONLY via onSave (no onBlur/auto-save, confirmed by grep) — so an edit typed before a delete is stranded in draft and lost on unmount; the typed values remain visible in the inputs until navigate-away and any later keystroke re-enables Save, so the window is narrow but real and display-only.

### BUG-054 — [P2][security] Any trip member (incl. Relaxer) can fabricate settlements between two OTHER members, corrupting everyone's shared balance graph, and cannot undo their own

_security · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.72_

- **Files:** `src/routes/settlements.py:133-461`, `src/routes/settlements.py:233-238`, `src/routes/settlements.py:486-522`, `src/routes/data.py:1160-1184`
- **Symptom:** A malicious or careless accepted member of a shared trip (any role, including a Relaxer) can POST a settlement asserting `fromUserId=<member A>` paid `toUserId=<member B>` up to roughly the trip's total spend, even though the caller is neither party. Because /api/data now ships ALL of a trip's settlements to ALL members (MONEY-3 fix, data.py:1160-1184) and the client balance reducer applies them to the shared per-person balance map, the fabricated row shifts the suggested-payment graph for every member. The two real parties see a debt marked 'paid' that nobody paid (or an inverted balance). The injected row can only be deleted by the trip OWNER or by the named payer (from_user_id) — NOT by the third-party who recorded it (settlements.py:521) — so the innocent payer is left to clean up a settlement they never created, and a Relaxer attacker can keep re-injecting (30/min).
- **Root cause:** create_settlement() deliberately does not require the caller to be one of the two parties ('the caller does NOT have to be one of the two parties', settlements.py:144-152). The only gate is `_is_accepted_member(cursor, trip_id, user_id)` (line 233), which returns True for every role including Relaxer. The amount cap (total_spend\*1.01, line 305) bounds the size but not the act of fabrication. The delete authorization (line 521: `user_id != owner_id and user_id != row['from_user_id']`) excludes the recorder, so a third-party who records cannot retract it.
- **Repro:** 1. Users A (owner), B, C are members of trip T with €900 of expenses. 2. C (a Relaxer) calls POST /api/settlements {tripId:T, fromUserId:A, toUserId:B, amount:900, currency:'EUR'}. 3. Server accepts (C is an accepted member; 900 < total_spend cap). 4. On next /api/data poll, A and B both see the €900 'A paid B' settlement applied to the balance graph — debts they never agreed to. 5. C cannot delete it; only A (owner) or A (payer) can. B (the falsely-credited recipient) also cannot delete it (recipient-can't-delete rule).
- **Suggested fix:** Restrict who can RECORD a settlement to: the payer, the recipient, or a planner/owner (drop Relaxer and drop arbitrary-third-party). At minimum, allow the third-party RECORDER to also delete the row they created (add `or user_id == row['recorded_by']` to the delete gate), so a mistaken/abusive injection is self-cleanable. Consider notifying BOTH parties (not just the recipient) when a non-party records a settlement, so the payer learns of a debt logged in their name.

### BUG-055 — [P2][bug] Revoked creator can no longer delete their own Trip Templates (delete gated on is_creator before ownership)

_settings · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `src/routes/templates.py:482`, `src/routes/templates.py:486`, `src/routes/templates.py:488`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Creator.tsx:104`
- **Symptom:** When an admin revokes a user's Creator status, that user's previously-published templates stay live (intended), but the user can no longer DELETE them — the delete call 403s. The Creator card disappears for them anyway, and even if reached, deletion fails with a generic 'save error' toast. There is also no admin UI to delete another user's templates, so revoked-creator templates become permanently un-removable through the product.
- **Root cause:** delete_template (templates.py:482) checks `if not _is_creator(cursor, user_id): return 403` (line 486) BEFORE running the ownership-scoped `DELETE … WHERE id=? AND owner_id=?` (line 488). Deleting your OWN content should require ownership, not the (separately revocable) can-CREATE privilege. set_creator (admin.py) only flips the flag and intentionally leaves templates live, but combined with this gate the user is locked out of managing their own published content after revocation.
- **Repro:** 1) As admin, grant user U creator. 2) U publishes a template T. 3) As admin, revoke U's creator (Developer → Make/Revoke). 4) As U, call DELETE /api/templates/<T> (or, before the card vanishes, tap Delete) → 403 Forbidden; T stays live forever with no way for U or the admin to remove it via the UI.
- **Suggested fix:** In delete_template, drop the \_is_creator gate and rely solely on the ownership-scoped DELETE (owner_id = user_id) + the existing 404-on-rowcount-0. Owning a template should be sufficient to delete it regardless of current creator status. (Create/update can keep the creator gate.)

### BUG-056 — [P2][bug] Cloned to-do places keep dangling dayId/timeOfDay pointing at the source trip's days — invisible on every per-day map view (sibling of the just-fixed template bug)

_sharing · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.90_

- **Files:** `src/routes/trips.py:1307`, `src/routes/trips.py:1309`, `src/routes/templates.py:85`, `src/routes/templates.py:106`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:183`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:143`
- **Symptom:** After cloning a trip, marked ('to-do') places that the source owner had pinned to a specific day no longer appear on that day in the clone. On the home map, when the user selects a numbered day, the cloned to-do markers vanish; they only show under the Anchor/overview, never carry a 'Day N' chip, and never surface in the cloned day's path panes. The to-do is effectively orphaned to a phantom day.
- **Root cause:** \_clone_trip_record copies marked_places_json VERBATIM (trips.py:1307-1309) while generating brand-new day ids for the cloned days (trips.py:1393, 1414). MarkedPlace.dayId (and AI timeOfDay) therefore reference the SOURCE trip's day ids, which do not exist in the clone. todoMarkers.ts:183 hides any place whose dayId != selectedDayId when on a numbered day, and the day chip lookup days.find(d => d.id === place.dayId) (todoMarkers.ts:143) returns nothing. This is the exact bug just fixed for Trip Templates, where \_clean_marked_places (templates.py:85-109) strips dayId/timeOfDay precisely because 'a trip created from a template has brand-new day ids ... those references are dangling'. The clone path was never given the same cleaning.
- **Repro:** 1) As owner, add a to-do place and assign it to Day 2 of a trip (or accept an AI plan that day-pins places). 2) Share the trip and clone it (or use /api/trips/clone). 3) Open the cloned trip's home map, select Day 2 on the path wheel → the to-do marker is gone. 4) Select Anchor → it reappears but with no 'Day 2' chip; it never shows in any day's plan pane.
- **Suggested fix:** Apply the same strip as templates.\_clean_marked_places when cloning: before writing src['marked_places_json'] into the new trip, json.loads it, drop dayId and timeOfDay from every entry, and re-dump. Factor templates.\_clean_marked_places into a shared helper and call it from \_clone_trip_record so the two paths can't drift again.
- **Verifier:** \_clone_trip_attempt copies src['marked_places_json'] verbatim (trips.py:1309) while cloned days get freshly generated ids (trips.py:1393/1414), and the clone path never calls \_clean_marked_places (which templates.py:106-107 uses to strip dayId/timeOfDay for exactly this dangling-id reason); todoMarkers.ts:183 skips any dayId-bearing place whose dayId != selectedDayId on per-day views and the chip lookup days.find(d=>d.id===place.dayId) (todoMarkers.ts:143) returns nothing, so cloned to-dos are hidden from the numbered day they point at and can't be re-slotted.

### BUG-057 — [P2][bug] Clone references the source owner's cover file; the clone's cover 404s when the original owner deletes their trip or changes the cover

_sharing · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.82_

- **Files:** `src/routes/trips.py:1320`, `src/routes/trips.py:1292`, `src/helpers.py:78`, `src/helpers.py:121`, `src/routes/trips.py:347`, `src/routes/trips.py:455`
- **Symptom:** A cloned trip's cover photo silently turns into a broken image when the original owner later deletes their source trip (or removes/replaces the cover). The cloner did nothing wrong and gets no warning; their trip card and hero just render a broken/empty cover.
- **Root cause:** \_clone_trip_attempt copies src['cover_url'] verbatim (trips.py:1320), so the clone's cover_url points at the ORIGINAL owner's uploaded file under /static/uploads/<owner_id>/<file>. When the owner deletes their trip, delete_trip collects that exact path (collect_trip_upload_paths includes cover_url, helpers.py:78-80) and delete_upload_files physically os.remove()s it (helpers.py:121-163, called at trips.py:455) with NO check for other trips/clones still referencing the file. The same break occurs on cover removal/replacement via upsert_trip. Files are also served read-any to signed-in users, so this is purely a dangling-reference/availability bug, but the clone permanently depends on an asset it doesn't own.
- **Repro:** 1) Owner A shares a trip that has an uploaded cover photo. 2) User B clones it via the share page. 3) B sees the cover correctly (it loads A's file). 4) A deletes the source trip (or Edit Trip → Remove cover). 5) B's cloned trip cover is now a broken image (the underlying /static/uploads/<A>/<file> is gone).
- **Suggested fix:** On clone, copy the cover bytes into the new owner's namespace (duplicate the file to /static/uploads/<new_owner_id>/<new_name> and store that path), so the clone owns its own asset. Alternatively, before delete_upload_files removes a cover/photo path, check whether any other trip row still references it and skip those. The copy-on-clone approach is cleaner and also fixes the cross-user file-ownership smell.
- **Verifier:** \_clone_trip_attempt copies src['cover_url'] verbatim (trips.py:1319) so the clone points at /static/uploads/<owner_id>/<file>; delete_trip snapshots cover_url via collect_trip_upload_paths (helpers.py:78-80) and physically os.remove()s it via delete_upload_files (trips.py:455, helpers.py:155-159) scoped to the OWNER's namespace with no cross-trip reference check, so the owner deleting their trip (or replacing the cover via the unconditional cover_url=excluded.cover_url upsert) leaves the clone's cover a dangling 404.

### BUG-058 — [P2][security] 401 session-expiry re-persists the logged-out user's trips to localStorage (privacy wipe defeated by the same handler's emit)

_state · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.83_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/api/core.ts:82`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/core.ts:269`, `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:353`, `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:369`, `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:438`
- **Symptom:** After a session silently expires/is-invalidated (token_jti bump from logout-elsewhere, 30-day expiry, deleted user), the next API 401 is supposed to wipe the cached state blob so a shared device doesn't leak the previous user's trips. The blob is removed — then re-written ~250ms later still containing User A's trips/expenses/budgets/days/archived trips. On the next boot at the login wall, loadState() reloads User A's data into STATE; if User B then signs in on that device there is a window where B's UI (trip selector, home map, collections) shows A's trips before pullFromServer overwrites them.
- **Root cause:** clearAuthToken() (api/core.ts:82) does localStorage.removeItem('theGreatEscapeState') and resets a SUBSET of STATE (notifications, draftExpense, geminiApiKey, settlements, achievements, lastImportBatch, preferences, rateMode, insightCurrency) but NOT the heavy domain arrays (STATE.trips/expenses/budgets/tripDays/archivedTrips/categories). The 401 branch in apiFetch (api/core.ts:269-284) calls clearAuthToken() then STATE.user=null then emit(EVENTS.STATE_CHANGED). The default subscriber `subscribe(EVENTS.STATE_CHANGED, saveState)` (state.ts:438) schedules a debounced \_doSave() (state.ts:353-367) which JSON.stringify(STATE)s the WHOLE object — including the trips still in memory — back into the key clearAuthToken just removed. The full logout path (pages/profile.ts:70-89) clears these arrays itself, which is why it's safe; the 401 + restoreSession()-failure callers of clearAuthToken (api/core.ts:275, bootstrap/auth.ts:193) rely on clearAuthToken to do the wipe, and it doesn't finish the job.
- **Repro:** 1. User A logs in on a shared browser; create a trip + expenses (now in STATE and localStorage). 2. Invalidate A's session server-side (log out from another device, or wait for token expiry) WITHOUT clicking Logout in this tab. 3. Trigger any API call (poll fires every 15s) → it 401s. 4. Inspect localStorage 'theGreatEscapeState' ~300ms later: A's trips/expenses are present again with user:null. 5. Reload → login wall, but STATE/localStorage still hold A's trips. 6. User B signs in → A's trips flash in the selector/home/collections until the first pull lands.
- **Suggested fix:** Make clearAuthToken() the single authoritative client wipe: reset the heavy domain arrays too (STATE.trips=[]; STATE.archivedTrips=[]; STATE.expenses=[]; STATE.budgets=[]; STATE.tripDays=[]; STATE.categories=[]; STATE.activeTripId=null) so the post-401 emit re-persists an EMPTY state. Alternatively, cancel the pending \_saveTimer inside clearAuthToken (clearTimeout(\_saveTimer)) AND guard \_doSave to skip writing when STATE.user is null after a wipe. Folding profile.ts's logout array-clears into clearAuthToken removes the duplication and closes every caller at once.
- **Verifier:** Verified core.ts:82-157 clearAuthToken removeItem's the blob but never resets STATE.trips/expenses/budgets/tripDays/archivedTrips/categories, and the 401 branch (core.ts:269-284) calls it then emit(STATE_CHANGED) which fires the saveState subscriber (state.ts:438) → debounced \_doSave JSON.stringify(STATE) (state.ts:363) re-writing A's trips back to the key just removed; downgraded from P1 because pullFromServer unconditionally reassigns STATE.trips (api.ts:183) so B never sees A's trips after their pull — the leak is a transient on-disk/first-paint window on a shared device, not persistent exposure or data loss.

### BUG-059 — [P2][correctness] Warm-path 409 union-merge resurrects a peer device's deleted media item

_state · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/api/media.ts:62`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/media.ts:107`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/media.ts:139`
- **Symptom:** User deletes a marked place / checklist item / photo on device A. Around the same time device B (which still has that item) edits the same trip's media. B's write 409s; the server echoes the current media (already without the deleted item); B's handler unions the server set with B's local snapshot (which still contains the item), so the deleted item reappears and is written back — the delete is silently undone for everyone.
- **Root cause:** \_postTripMedia's 409 recovery (media.ts:139-144) re-merges via \_mergeMediaField (media.ts:62-73), a pure union-by-key that keeps any key present on EITHER side. The cold/parked path's loss-free claim relies on 'the only possible offline edit is an ADD' (media.ts:46), but the warm 409 path runs on a fully-hydrated trip where a DELETE is a normal edit. Union-by-key cannot represent a deletion, so a concurrent delete always loses to any concurrent edit. There is no tombstone/per-item version to distinguish 'never had it' from 'deleted it'.
- **Repro:** Open the same trip on two logged-in devices, both with marked place P loaded. On A, remove P from the To-do list (persists). On B, before B re-pulls, add a different place Q (triggers a media write that 409s and merges). Re-open the trip on A → P is back.
- **Suggested fix:** Add per-item soft-delete tombstones (e.g. a deletedAt set the server retains for a window) so \_mergeMediaField can drop a server item the local side tombstoned, and drop a local item the server tombstoned — instead of unconditionally keeping the union. At minimum, document this as a known last-writer-wins-for-deletes limitation and surface a 'trip media changed on another device' toast on a 409 merge so the user can verify.
- **Verifier:** \_postTripMedia's 409 recovery (media.ts:128-159) re-merges via \_mergeMediaField (media.ts:62-73), a pure union-by-key with no tombstone, and persistTripMedia/upsertTrip send the full current media snapshot on every edit (api.ts:499) so a local DELETE is just an absent key — when the write 409s the server's current copy (which still has the item) re-adds it, undoing the delete; real correctness bug on a hydrated trip under a concurrent-edit version conflict, bounded to resurrecting one media item.

### BUG-060 — [P2][bug] Service worker calls skipWaiting() on every install — the 'Update available, reload?' prompt is dead code and tabs auto-reload mid-edit

_sync-offline · verdict: **uncertain** · confidence 0.86_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/sw.js:89`, `frontend/static/sw.js:104`, `frontend/static/js/src/main.ts:443`, `frontend/static/js/src/main.ts:394`, `frontend/static/js/src/main.ts:429`
- **Symptom:** On a deploy with an SW version bump, every open tab/PWA window reloads itself WITHOUT asking — wiping any unsaved form input (a half-typed expense, trip note, journal entry). The branded 'Update available — Reload?' confirm modal users were supposed to see never appears. First-ever visit also does one extra full reload.
- **Root cause:** install handler unconditionally calls `self.skipWaiting()` (sw.js:89) and activate calls `self.clients.claim()` (sw.js:104). skipWaiting promotes the new SW straight past the 'waiting' state, so `registration.waiting` is (almost) never populated — and the entire tryPrompt/showConfirmModal flow in main.ts:394-431 gates on `registration.waiting`, so it never fires. Instead clients.claim() triggers `controllerchange`, and main.ts:443-447 reloads immediately (guarded only by a once-flag, with no `navigator.serviceWorker.controller` first-install check), so updates apply with a surprise reload and first load double-loads.
- **Repro:** 1. Load the app, type into the expense form but don't save. 2. Deploy a new sw.js (bump SW_VERSION) — or trigger reg.update() via bfcache pageshow (main.ts:456). 3. New SW installs → skipWaiting → activate → claim → controllerchange → window.location.reload(). 4. The tab reloads and the typed input is gone; no prompt was shown.
- **Suggested fix:** Remove the unconditional skipWaiting() from install; let the SW sit in 'waiting' so main.ts's updatefound→tryPrompt→(user accepts)→postMessage('SKIP_WAITING') flow drives activation. Keep the SKIP_WAITING message handler (sw.js:464). Also guard the controllerchange reload so it doesn't reload on first install (when there was no prior controller).
- **Verifier:** Plausible and the cited mechanism (skipWaiting + clients.claim defeating a registration.waiting-gated prompt) is a known pattern, but I did not re-read the main.ts update-prompt gating to fully confirm.

### BUG-061 — [P2][bug] Outbox is never drained on the 15s poll or on tab re-focus — a mutation that fails while ONLINE (e.g. a 20s timeout) stays stuck until the next offline→online transition or a full reload

_sync-offline · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.82_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/main.ts:317`, `frontend/static/js/src/main.ts:261`, `frontend/static/js/src/main.ts:283`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/core.ts:218`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/core.ts:251`
- **Symptom:** A write that fails transiently while the user is online and STAYS online (slow 3G causing the 20s AbortSignal.timeout to fire, which apiFetch treats as a network failure and enqueues) is never replayed: it sits in the outbox until the browser fires an `online` event (which won't happen if connectivity never actually dropped) or the page is reloaded. The user's edit appears locally but never reaches the server, and gets dropped on the next pull.
- **Root cause:** drainOutbox() is only invoked from the `online` event listener (main.ts:319) and a one-shot 2s boot timer (main.ts:333). The recurring 15s poll (main.ts:261-269) calls only syncWithServer + fetchNotifications, and the visibilitychange/pageshow handlers (main.ts:283-301) likewise never drain. apiFetch enqueues on ANY caught failure including the 20s timeout (core.ts:218,251), so an online-but-slow request becomes a stuck queue item with no trigger to retry.
- **Repro:** 1. Stay online but on a very slow link. 2. Save an expense; the request exceeds 20s and aborts → enqueued. 3. Link recovers but no offline→online edge ever fired. 4. The expense never replays; it disappears on the next pullFromServer.
- **Suggested fix:** Also call drainOutbox() from the 15s poll tick (guarded by pendingCount()>0 and the existing \_draining mutex) and/or on visibilitychange when the tab regains focus, so online-but-transient failures get retried without requiring a connectivity edge or reload.
- **Verifier:** Matches the architecture: drainOutbox is wired only to the 'online' event + a one-shot boot timer; the recurring poll and visibility handlers call sync/notifications but not drain, while apiFetch enqueues on any failure including the online 20s timeout.

### BUG-062 — [P2][data-loss] drainOutbox drops a 4xx (401/403) replay silently with no user feedback — offline edits by a since-demoted/kicked member, or after session expiry, vanish without a toast

_sync-offline · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.74_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/outbox.ts:369`, `frontend/static/js/src/outbox.ts:377`
- **Symptom:** If a planner edits a trip's expenses/days offline and, during the offline window, the owner demotes them to viewer or removes them (or their session expires), the replayed writes return 403/401 and are dropped silently with only a console.warn. The user's offline work is gone and they're never told.
- **Root cause:** \_drainOutboxImpl treats any 4xx other than 409 as a permanent client error and removes the item with only `console.warn` (outbox.ts:369-380). Unlike the inline upsert path (which toasts staleEdit on 409 and clears the session on 401 via apiFetch), the drain path has no user-facing surface, so the loss is invisible.
- **Repro:** 1. As a trip planner, go offline and edit several days/expenses. 2. Have the owner demote you to viewer (or let your session expire). 3. Reconnect → drain replays → server 403/401 → items dropped with no toast; your edits never persisted and you get no notice.
- **Suggested fix:** On a dropped 4xx during drain (especially 401/403), surface a one-time toast ('Some offline changes couldn't be saved — your access changed') and/or trigger pullFromServer so the UI reflects the rejected state. For 401 specifically, route through the same session-cleared handling as apiFetch.
- **Verifier:** Verified inline at outbox.ts:369-380: any 4xx other than 409 is removed from the queue with only console.warn and no user-facing toast or pull.

### BUG-063 — [P2][bug] Instantiated template (and clone) day rows keep NULL dates that never populate when the new owner sets a trip date range

_templates · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `src/routes/templates.py:273-303`, `src/routes/trips.py:1395-1417`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:518-594`
- **Symptom:** A user creates a trip from a template that included a day-by-day plan, then opens Edit Trip and picks a date range (e.g. Jul 1–5). The trip-level dates save, but the individual day cards on the home Path stay date-less forever — no day shows a date, 'today' highlighting never lights up, and any date-keyed feature (photo/day bucketing, calendar ordering, PDF day dates) stays blank. The dates appear to 'not stick' to the itinerary.
- **Root cause:** \_instantiate_template inserts every day with date=NULL (templates.py:285,290) — by design, matching \_clone_trip_record which NULLs dates and whose comment (trips.py:1395-1406) explicitly states the frontend is supposed to populate fresh dates when the new owner picks a start. But the Edit-Trip date logic can't do that: it pre-fills the picker from numberedDays[0].date (trip.ts:319) which is '' for an instantiated trip, and its rebase/extend branches are gated on `startChanged = newStart && oldFirst && ...` / `endChanged = newEnd && oldLast && ...` (trip.ts:532-535). oldFirst/oldLast come from parseUTC(numberedDays[0|N].date || '') which is null when the days have no dates, so both guards short-circuit to false and NO date is ever written to the day rows (the only path that scaffolds fresh dates is the numberedDays.length===0 branch, which doesn't apply here because the days exist). The documented clone/template date-assignment contract is therefore broken for both clone and template instantiation.
- **Repro:** 1) Create a template with 'Day plans' included from a multi-day trip, OR clone any multi-day trip. 2) Open the new trip's Edit Trip modal. 3) Pick a start+end date range and Save. 4) Go to Home -> Path: the day cards still show no dates; reopening Edit Trip shows the date picker blank again. Trip.dateFrom/dateTo are set but the trip_days rows remain date=NULL.
- **Suggested fix:** In modals/trip.ts, add a case for 'numbered days exist but have no dates': when oldFirst is null (or any numbered day lacks a date) and the user supplies a start, assign dates sequentially from the new start (day N gets start + (dayNumber-1)) and push them to `rebased` so they persist via upsertDay. Equivalently, treat a fully-date-less numbered set like the scaffold-from-scratch path but keep the existing day ids/plan content.
- **Verifier:** Confirmed \_instantiate_template inserts every day with date=NULL (templates.py:285), and in Edit Trip numberedDays filters dayNumber>0 (trip.ts:312-313) so dateless instantiated days take the else-branch (not the length===0 scaffold path); prefill is numberedDays[0].date||'' = '' (trip.ts:319), so oldFirst/oldLast=parseUTC('')=null (trip.ts:527-528) and startChanged/endChanged short-circuit to false (trip.ts:532-535), so no date is ever written to the day rows — finalizeAndClose only sets trip.dateFrom/dateTo and persists scaffolded/rebased/renumbered, none of which carry a fresh date (trip.ts:601-621); no data loss, only degraded per-day dates, hence P2.

### BUG-064 — [P2][data-loss] Two distinct marked places that share a name collide in the media merge — one is silently dropped (wrong dedup key)

_todo · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.83_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/api/media.ts:52`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/media.ts:62`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/media.ts:142`, `frontend/static/js/src/markedPlaces.ts:109`, `frontend/static/js/src/markedPlaces.ts:296`
- **Symptom:** On any media merge (a 409 concurrent-edit conflict, or the cold-window park-and-flush), two genuinely different marked places that happen to share the same display name (extremely common with chains — two 'Starbucks', two 'McDonald's', two 'Pharmacy', two 'Hotel Ibis') get deduped down to a single entry. The user loses one place from their to-do list / map without any indication.
- **Root cause:** \_mergeMediaField dedups by `_mediaKey(item)` = `String(o.id ?? o.url ?? o.name ?? JSON.stringify(item))`. A MarkedPlace's canonical identity is `placeId` (the type's `id`/`url` fields are NEVER populated — neither toggleTodoListMembership (markedPlaces.ts:109) nor addOrUpdatePlaceFromVerified (markedPlaces.ts:296) sets `id` or `url`). So `_mediaKey` falls through to `name`, and two different placeIds with the same name map to the same key — the second is treated as a duplicate and discarded. (Nameless items, e.g. an AI item with empty text/verifiedName, all collapse to key '' too.)
- **Repro:** Empirically reproduced: `_mergeMediaField([{placeId:'A',name:'Starbucks'}], [{placeId:'A',name:'Starbucks'},{placeId:'B',name:'Starbucks'}])` returns only `[{placeId:'A'}]` — place B is dropped. In product terms: have two same-named places in the to-do list, trigger a media merge (edit the same trip's media from a 2nd device to force a 409, or add during the cold window), and one Starbucks vanishes.
- **Suggested fix:** Make \_mediaKey aware of the per-collection identity: prefer `placeId` for marked places (e.g. `o.placeId ?? o.id ?? o.url ?? o.name ?? JSON.stringify(item)`), or pass a per-field key extractor into \_mergeMediaField so markedPlaces key on placeId, photos/documents on url, checklist on id.

### BUG-065 — [P2][correctness] Accept Plan orphans manually-pinned places' dayId — they silently disappear from every day's pane and per-day map markers

_todo · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/ai/useAiPlan.ts:450`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/ai/useAiPlan.ts:466`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:348`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:183`, `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:262`
- **Symptom:** A user adds a place from the home map while viewing 'Day 3' (toggleTodoListMembership auto-pins it to that day's id). Later they generate and Accept an AI plan. The place stays in the to-do list, but it no longer appears in any day's 'pinned to this slot' strip in the Day Detail modal, and it no longer shows on the map when a specific day is selected — its day pin was silently lost.
- **Root cause:** onAcceptPlan() deletes ALL existing numbered days (useAiPlan.ts:450-456) and creates brand-new ones with fresh ids `'day_'+Date.now()+'_'+idx` (useAiPlan.ts:466). dropAITaggedPlaces only removes source:'ai' entries, so a manual place survives — but it keeps its OLD dayId, which now matches no existing day. dayDetailModal.\_renderPlacesForSlot filters by `p.dayId === day.id` (dayDetailModal.ts:351) so it never matches; todoMarkers.ts:183-186 filters it out of every numbered-day view. There is no orphaned-dayId healing: state.ts only migrates documents/photos `dayId:null→anchorId` (state.ts:262-270), never validates markedPlaces.dayId against existing days.
- **Repro:** 1. On the home map, select Day 3 on the path wheel. 2. Open a POI InfoWindow and click 'Add to to-do' (the place is pinned to Day 3). 3. Go to AI, generate a plan, Accept it. 4. Open any day's Detail modal — the place is gone from the slot strips; select a numbered day on the map — its to-do marker is gone. It only reappears in the Anchor (all-days) view.
- **Suggested fix:** On Accept Plan, remap or clear stale dayIds: after building the new days, null out any surviving markedPlace.dayId that doesn't match a current day (so it falls back to the trip-wide Anchor view), or add an orphaned-dayId sweep in loadState/fetchTripMedia that nulls markedPlace.dayId values with no matching TripDay.

### BUG-066 — [P2][bug] Failed trip DELETE silently swallowed — trip vanishes then reappears on next poll with no error

_trips · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.88_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/bootstrap/trip-controls.ts:174-207`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections/handlers.ts:116-143`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:504-507`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/core.ts:302-306`
- **Symptom:** User clicks Delete on a trip. The trip immediately disappears from the UI. If the server DELETE actually fails (500, transient 5xx, or a 403 because ownership changed), no error is shown — and ~15s later, on the next /api/data poll, the deleted trip silently reappears in their list. The user believes they deleted it; it comes back like a ghost.
- **Root cause:** deleteTrip() -> \_delete() (core.ts:302) calls apiFetch(...).catch(e=>console.error). apiFetch only THROWS on network-level failures (it returns the Response for any HTTP status, including 4xx/5xx). So a 500/403 is a resolved promise with res.ok=false. Neither deleteActiveTrip (trip-controls.ts:200-204) nor deleteArchivedTrip (handlers.ts:135-139) ever inspects res.ok — they only `catch` (which never fires for an HTTP error) and then navigate. Meanwhile delete_trip server-side only writes the trip_deletes tombstone INSIDE the transaction (trips.py:443), so a failed delete leaves no tombstone and the row persists. pullFromServer does `STATE.trips = allTrips.filter(...)` (api.ts:183) — a full replace from the server — so the still-existing trip is re-added. The optimistic local removal is undone with zero user feedback.
- **Repro:** 1. Own a trip. 2. Force the DELETE to return non-2xx (e.g. server 500, or revoke ownership server-side so it 403s). 3. Click Delete and confirm. 4. Observe trip disappears. 5. Wait ~15s for the next /api/data poll (or reload). 6. The trip reappears with no error toast — user is confused.
- **Suggested fix:** Make deleteTrip/\_delete return a result the caller checks: if !res.ok, re-insert the optimistically-removed trip into STATE (or skip the optimistic removal until success) and show a localized 'Couldn’t delete — try again' toast. Mirror the await-then-check pattern the expense/day flows use. The same fix applies to deleteArchivedTrip.
- **Verifier:** Verified \_delete (core.ts:302-306) only .catch()es, deleteActiveTrip (trip-controls.ts:200-204) and deleteArchivedTrip (handlers.ts:135-139) never inspect res.ok, apiFetch returns Response for 4xx/5xx without throwing, server writes the trip_deletes tombstone + DELETE only inside the committed txn (trips.py:436-450), and pullFromServer full-replaces STATE.trips (api.ts:183) — so a failed delete silently un-removes the trip with no user feedback; not data-loss (nothing destroyed) so P2.

### BUG-067 — [P2][data-loss] Failed trip CREATE (daily cap 429 / 500) is silently swallowed; new trip is lost on next poll

_trips · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.83_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:226-231`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:483-501`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:419`, `src/routes/trips.py:127-133`
- **Symptom:** After hitting Create, the trip appears locally. But if the server rejects the create (the per-user 50/day trip-create cap returns 429 with {userCapHit:true}, or any 500), the user gets NO error. The trip lives only in local STATE and quietly disappears on the next /api/data poll — all the day scaffolding and the just-created trip are gone with no explanation.
- **Root cause:** openNewTripModal’s submit does `try { await upsertTrip(newTrip); await Promise.all(scaffolded.map(upsertDay)) } catch { /* outbox retries */ } navigate('home')`. upsertTrip -> \_upsertWithUpdatedAt returns {ok:false,status:429|500,...} WITHOUT throwing for any HTTP response (api.ts:419 returns the envelope; only network errors throw). So the catch never fires and the return value is ignored. The outbox is only populated in apiFetch’s network-failure catch (core.ts:236-256), so a 429/500 is NOT queued for retry. On the next pull, STATE.trips is fully replaced from the server (api.ts:183), which has no such trip → it vanishes. Note the AI-plan flow explicitly handles userCapHit (useAiPlan.ts:370) but the trip-create flow does not.
- **Repro:** 1. As one user, create 50 trips in a day (hits the trips.py:129 cap). 2. Create a 51st trip via New Trip modal. 3. Observe it appears locally with no error. 4. Wait for the next poll/reload → the trip and its scaffolded days are gone silently. (Same outcome for any 500 on the create POST.)
- **Suggested fix:** Inspect the upsertTrip result: on !ok (esp. 429/userCapHit) roll back the optimistic STATE.trips/tripDays push and show a localized error ('Daily new-trip limit reached' / 'Couldn’t save trip'). Reuse the userCapHit handling pattern already in useAiPlan.ts.
- **Verifier:** Verified server returns 429 {userCapHit:true} at trips.py:127-133, \_upsertWithUpdatedAt returns {ok:false} without throwing on any HTTP error (api.ts:419), the create handler's catch never fires and ignores the return value (trip.ts:227-231), enqueueMutation only runs in apiFetch's network-failure catch (core.ts:251) so a 429/500 is never queued, and pullFromServer full-replaces STATE.trips (api.ts:183) dropping the optimistic trip — but the trip was never persisted so this is a lost-unsaved-draft UX failure, not destruction of saved data, hence P2.

### BUG-068 — [P2][bug] Cloned trip's marked places keep the SOURCE trip's dayId → wishlist pins become invisible on every day filter

_trips · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `src/routes/trips.py:1281-1320 (_clone_trip_attempt)`, `src/routes/trips.py:1309`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:183-186`, `src/routes/templates.py:104-107`
- **Symptom:** Clone a trip (via 'I want this trip' / public clone). On the new copy, marked places that were attached to a specific day in the original do not appear as map pins on any day view — they’re effectively orphaned. The exact same content imported via a Template DOES show correctly, so cloning silently degrades the wishlist relative to templates.
- **Root cause:** \_clone_trip_attempt copies src['marked_places_json'] VERBATIM (trips.py:1309) while generating brand-new day ids for the clone’s trip_days. So each cloned marked place still carries dayId pointing at a SOURCE-trip day that does not exist in the clone. In todoMarkers.ts the day filter does: if (!selectedIsAnchor && place.dayId && place.dayId !== selectedDayId) continue (line 183) and if (!selectedIsAnchor && !place.dayId) continue (line 186). A place with a dangling dayId never equals any real day in the clone, so it’s skipped on every numbered-day view, AND because it HAS a dayId it’s skipped on the Anchor view too → invisible everywhere. The template snapshot path explicitly strips dayId/timeOfDay for exactly this reason (templates.py:106-107); the clone path never got the same treatment.
- **Repro:** 1. On trip A, mark a place and assign it to Day 2. 2. Clone trip A (clone_trip or clone_trip_from_share_token). 3. Open the cloned trip’s home map. 4. Select any day, and the Anchor — the cloned marked place pin appears on none of them.
- **Suggested fix:** In \_clone_trip_attempt, parse marked_places_json and null out (or drop) dayId (and timeOfDay) on each entry before storing, mirroring templates.py’s \_strip. Optionally remap dayId via an old→new day-id map built during the day-copy loop, but null-to-trip-wide matches the template contract and is simplest.
- **Verifier:** \_clone_trip_attempt copies src['marked_places_json'] verbatim (trips.py:1309) and grep confirms \_clean_marked_places is called ONLY on the template path (templates.py:185,220), never in the clone path, while clone generates fresh day ids (trips.py:1393) and NULLs day dates — so cloned to-do pins carry dangling source dayIds that todoMarkers.ts:183 skips on numbered days and todoMarkers.ts:186 skips on Anchor view, making them invisible on the map (they still list on /todo), a real bug at P2.

### BUG-069 — [P2][bug] Background /api/data poll replaces STATE.trips while the Edit-Trip modal is open, detaching the edited object

_trips · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:183-184`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:335-341`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:243-247`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:452-463`
- **Symptom:** If a 15s background poll lands while the user has the Edit Trip modal open, their pending edits can flash away on save (the UI briefly shows the pre-edit values), and in a true concurrent-edit case the save is rejected with a 'stale edit' toast even though the user didn’t do anything wrong.
- **Root cause:** openEditTripModal captures a reference to a specific STATE.trips object (trip.ts:243). pullFromServer unconditionally does `STATE.trips = allTrips.filter(...)` (api.ts:183) — building brand-new objects — even when a modal is open; the modal-open guard at api.ts:335-336 only suppresses the re-NAVIGATE, not the STATE replacement. So mid-edit the modal’s `trip` becomes an orphan no longer in STATE. On submit, the modal mutates the detached object and emits state:changed (which re-renders from the fresh STATE objects, momentarily dropping the user’s edits), then upsertTrip(detached) sends the change with the updatedAt captured at modal-open. If anyone touched the trip server-side in between, that stamp is stale → 409 staleEdit toast (api.ts:413) for a single-editor user.
- **Repro:** 1. Open Edit Trip on a trip and start typing a new name (leave the modal open ~15s so a poll lands). 2. Save. 3. Observe a brief flash where the old name shows before the write round-trips. 4. Variant: have a second device rename the same trip during the window → saving the first device shows a confusing 'stale edit' toast.
- **Suggested fix:** Either pause/skip the STATE.trips reassignment in pullFromServer when a modal is open (extend the existing modalOpen guard to the state apply, not just navigate), or have edit modals re-resolve the live STATE.trips object by id at submit time and merge field-by-field instead of holding a captured reference.
- **Verifier:** openEditTripModal takes a STATE.trips reference (invoked with activeTrip at TripBody.tsx:522) and mutates it in place (trip.ts:452-463), while pullFromServer unconditionally rebuilds STATE.trips = allTrips.filter(...) with brand-new objects (api.ts:183) and the modalOpen guard only suppresses the re-navigate at api.ts:335-336 not the STATE replacement — so a mid-edit poll orphans the modal's trip; the edit is still POSTed (no data loss) but causes a render flash and an edge-case stale-stamp 409 only if the trip was also touched server-side, so P2.

## P3 (35)

### BUG-070 — [P3][bug] Budget card "was X" badge converts the original amount to home currency, destroying the foreign figure it exists to show (no-rate currencies show the raw number with the wrong symbol)

_budgets · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.92_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/budgets/Budgets.tsx:352-355`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/currency.ts:137-141`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:694-699`
- **Symptom:** A budget created in a foreign currency shows a wrong/meaningless "· was X" badge. For a USD-typed budget on a EUR home, the card reads "Target €86.10 · was €86.10" — the badge duplicates the target and shows euros, not the "$100" the user typed. For a non-EUR home it shows yet another converted number. Worst case: a no-rate currency (VND/EGP/ARS) budget shows "· was €500,000.00" — the raw foreign number stamped with the euro symbol, claiming a €18 budget "was" 500,000 euros.
- **Root cause:** Budgets.tsx:354 renders the original amount with `formatHome(b.originalAmount || 0, b.originalCurrency)`. `formatHome(amount, from)` converts `from`→the user's HOME currency and formats with the HOME symbol (currency.ts:137-141), discarding `b.originalCurrency` entirely. The badge's whole purpose (per the `originalAmount`/`originalCurrency` columns and budgets.py:89-96) is to preserve the user-typed foreign amount. The badge only renders when `b.originalCurrency !== 'EUR'` (line 353), so it is ALWAYS wrong when shown. For no-rate currencies `convertCurrency` falls back to rate=1 (currency.ts:71-78), so the foreign number passes through unscaled but gets the home symbol. The server-side PDF renderer gets this right — it uses `tr.money(orig_curr, orig_amount)` (pdf/**init**.py:696-697) — proving the intended behavior; the web card diverged.
- **Repro:** 1) Home currency = EUR. 2) Budgets → New budget, pick USD, enter 100, save. 3) Card shows "Target €86.10 · was €86.10" (badge is redundant + euros, not "$100.00"). 4) Now pick a no-rate currency (set currency to VND, enter the manual EUR target 18). 5) Card shows "Target €18.00 · was €500,000.00" — wrong symbol and a nonsensical figure.
- **Suggested fix:** Render the original amount in its OWN currency, not the home currency. Replace `formatHome(b.originalAmount || 0, b.originalCurrency)` with a direct format, e.g. `formatCurrency(b.originalAmount || 0, b.originalCurrency)` (i18n.ts) or `currencySymbol(b.originalCurrency) + formatNumberForCurrency(b.originalAmount || 0, b.originalCurrency)` — mirroring the PDF's `tr.money(orig_curr, orig_amount)` path.
- **Verifier:** Budgets.tsx:354 calls formatHome(b.originalAmount, b.originalCurrency); formatHome (currency.ts:138-140) converts from->home and formatCurrency (i18n) renders with the HOME code, so the parenthetical "was" badge shows a converted home value with the home symbol instead of the user-typed foreign amount, and no-rate currencies pass through unscaled with the wrong symbol (PDF **init**.py:697 does it right via tr.money) — but it is a cosmetic secondary badge, the canonical amount still renders correctly, no data loss.

### BUG-071 — [P3][bug] Account-wide ('all trips') budget is silently hidden and unrecoverable when the active trip is the only trip carrying budgets

_budgets · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/budgets/Budgets.tsx:45-54`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/budgets/Budgets.tsx:80-83`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:201`
- **Symptom:** A user who has one trip-scoped budget on their first/active trip AND an account-wide ('All trips') budget opens the Budgets page and sees ONLY the trip budget. The account-wide budget is missing from the list, from the count ("1 budget"), and from the Overall card — with no filter chip to reveal it and no way to clear the filter.
- **Root cause:** On mount the filter lazy-initializes to the active trip when that trip has any budget: `filterTrip = activeTripId && allBudgets.some(b => b.tripId === activeTripId) ? activeTripId : ''` (Budgets.tsx:46-50). `visibleBudgets` then filters to an EXACT tripId match (line 52-53), excluding tripId='all' budgets. The filter chips (including the "All trips" reset chip) only render when `tripsInBudgets.length > 1` (line 83), and `tripsInBudgets` excludes 'all' (line 80-81). So with budgets = [{tripId:'t1'},{tripId:'all'}] and active=t1: filterTrip='t1', showTripChips=false → the 'all' budget is filtered out with no UI to recover. `activeTripId` defaults to `STATE.trips[0].id` on every load (api.ts:201), so this state is common, not exotic.
- **Repro:** 1) Have exactly one trip (it becomes the active/first trip). 2) Create a budget scoped to that trip. 3) Create a second budget scoped to 'All trips'. 4) Navigate to Budgets. 5) Only the trip budget shows; count says "1 budget"; no filter chips appear; the account-wide budget is invisible with no way to reveal it.
- **Suggested fix:** Either (a) always include tripId='all' budgets in a per-trip filtered view (an account-wide cap applies to every trip), or (b) render the filter chips (incl. the "All trips" reset) whenever a filter is active OR there is more than one distinct scope — e.g. `showTripChips = tripsInBudgets.length > 1 || (filterTrip && allBudgets.some(b => b.tripId === 'all' || b.tripId !== filterTrip))` — so the user can always clear the auto-filter.
- **Verifier:** With budgets [{tripId:'t1'},{tripId:'all'}] and active=t1, the lazy init (Budgets.tsx:46-50) sets filterTrip='t1' (the .some matches), visibleBudgets (53) exact-matches tripId so the 'all' row is excluded, and tripsInBudgets (80-81) drops 'all' leaving length 1 so showTripChips=false (83) — no reset chip renders, so the 'all' budget is hidden on this page with no UI to clear the filter; but the data is intact (still in STATE/server, still shown in Insights via tripId==='all' at Insights.tsx:477) and recovers by adding/removing any budget, so impact is a hidden card not lost data.

### BUG-072 — [P3][correctness] Read side hard-assumes budget.amount is EUR and ignores the stored currency column — a non-EUR budget from the API/CSV-import/legacy path is misread as euros

_budgets · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/budgets/Budgets.tsx:352`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/budgets/helpers.ts:182,198,258`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/insights/Insights.tsx:480-481`, `src/routes/budgets.py:48-49,202-225`
- **Symptom:** If a budget is stored with a non-EUR `currency` and an `amount` denominated in that currency (e.g. amount=5000, currency='THB'), every frontend surface treats 5000 as euros: the card shows "Target €5,000", allocation/remaining math adds 5000 EUR, and spent-vs-budget compares against €5,000 — a large silent misread.
- **Root cause:** The EUR-canonical invariant for budget.amount is enforced ONLY by the create modal (helpers.ts:395-401 converts to EUR and forces `currency:'EUR'`). The server (budgets.py:48-49) stores `amount` and `currency` verbatim with NO server-side conversion to EUR, and the read serializer ships both (data.py:1205-1222). But the frontend NEVER reads `b.currency` anywhere — `allocatedAcrossBudgets`, `budgetStatus`, and both card renders all pass `b.amount` to `formatHome(..., 'EUR')`. So any write path other than the modal (the raw `/api/budgets` API, a future CSV import, or legacy data — all explicitly acknowledged as live paths in budgets.py:62-63) can desynchronize amount/currency from the EUR assumption and be misread.
- **Repro:** POST /api/budgets with `{budget:{id:…, amount:5000, currency:'THB', tripId:'all'}}` (passes server validation since THB has a live rate). The Budgets card renders "Target €5,000.00" and the Overall counts 5000 EUR, although the intent was 5000 THB (~€130).
- **Suggested fix:** Either normalize amount→EUR server-side in upsert_budget (convert `amount` from `currency` to EUR before storing, the way the modal does client-side), making the EUR invariant authoritative; or make the read side honor `b.currency` by converting `formatHome(convertCurrency(b.amount, b.currency, 'EUR'), 'EUR')`. Pick one source of truth so non-modal write paths can't misrepresent the target.
- **Verifier:** grep confirms b.currency is never read in Budgets.tsx/helpers.ts; amount is always passed to formatHome(..., 'EUR') (Budgets.tsx:352, helpers.ts:258, Insights.tsx:481) and budgetStatus uses budget.amount as EUR (helpers.ts:198), while the server stores amount/currency verbatim with no EUR conversion (budgets.py:48-49) and only rejects no-rate non-EUR (the IA-10 gate at budgets.py:64-71 still ACCEPTS e.g. currency:USD with a rate) — so a raw /api/budgets caller can desync amount from EUR; latent because the only first-party write path (the modal, helpers.ts:400) forces EUR and /api/sync now ignores budgets (data.py:791).

### BUG-073 — [P3][correctness] Budgeteers are mislabelled as 'Relaxer' on the trip header role badge

_companions · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.92_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/TripBody.tsx:647-654`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/TripBody.tsx:137-138`, `frontend/static/js/src/permissions.ts:49-59`
- **Symptom:** A member with the Budgeteer role (can add/edit expenses but not trip details) sees a '👁 Relaxer' (view-only) badge on the trip header, mislabelling their role and implying they can't edit anything — when in fact they can edit expenses.
- **Root cause:** The header renders the badge with `{!tripIsEditable ? <Relaxer badge> : null}` where `tripIsEditable = canEdit(activeTrip)` (TripBody.tsx:138), and `canEdit` is planner-only (permissions.ts:49-51). So for BOTH relaxers and budgeteers `tripIsEditable` is false, and the same hardcoded '👁 Relaxer' badge (companions.relaxerBadgeTitle / roleRelaxer) is shown. There is no branch for the budgeteer role.
- **Repro:** 1. Owner invites a friend as Budgeteer; friend accepts. 2. As the budgeteer, open the trip. 3. Header shows '👁 Relaxer' even though the expense form is editable for them.
- **Suggested fix:** Compute the badge from `getMyRole(activeTrip)`: show 'Planner' (or no badge) for planner, 'Budgeteer' for budgeteer, 'Relaxer' for relaxer, with role-appropriate title text. Reuse the same role-label switch already present in MemberChipsPanel.renderBadge.
- **Verifier:** TripBody.tsx:647-654 renders the hardcoded '👁 Relaxer' badge whenever `!tripIsEditable`, and tripIsEditable=canEdit (line 138) is planner-only (permissions.ts:49-51), so a budgeteer hits the relaxer branch with no budgeteer case — confirmed, but it's a cosmetic self-badge mislabel with no functional/permission impact (the chip panel labels budgeteers correctly at TripBody.tsx:928-936), hence P3.

### BUG-074 — [P3][correctness] Linking a friend to a same-named existing unlinked companion silently merges two different people

_companions · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.78_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/modals/companions.ts:358-365`, `frontend/static/js/src/companions.ts:45-57`, `frontend/static/js/src/companions.ts:144-150`
- **Symptom:** Owner has an unlinked companion 'Alex' (their non-app friend Alex P). Owner then adds an app-friend who is ALSO named 'Alex' (a different person, Alex M). Instead of creating a second entry, the existing 'Alex' row is promoted and linked to Alex M's account — so Alex M gets the invite and the trip now attributes Alex P's name/expenses to Alex M. The two people are conflated with no warning.
- **Root cause:** In the brand-new-add branch, `findTripCompanion(trip, friendName)` (companions.ts:360) matches purely by name, case-insensitively (companions.ts:45-57), and if an unlinked row exists it sets `existingByName.linkedUserId = friendId` (line 362). There is no check that the existing unlinked entry actually refers to the same person. Because `addTripCompanion` also dedupes by name (companions.ts:144-150), the roster can never hold two 'Alex' rows, forcing the merge.
- **Repro:** 1. In a trip, add an unlinked companion named 'Alex' via the inline form. 2. 'Add a friend' and pick a different friend whose display name is also 'Alex'. 3. The single 'Alex' row becomes linked to the friend; the originally-intended different 'Alex' is gone, and the friend receives the invite.
- **Suggested fix:** When promoting an existing unlinked row to a friend link, confirm with the owner ('There's already a companion named Alex — link this row to <friend>, or add a separate entry?'). Or disambiguate by appending a distinguishing tag (e.g. last-name initial) so two same-named people can coexist, instead of force-merging on name.
- **Verifier:** companions.ts (modal) :360-362 matches the friend's name case-insensitively via findTripCompanion (companions.ts:45-57) and sets existingByName.linkedUserId with no identity check, and addTripCompanion dedupes by name (companions.ts:146-150) so two same-name rows can't coexist — real but an edge case requiring a name collision, no data loss, so P3.

### BUG-075 — [P3][bug] Companion remove-lock is case-sensitive while the rest of the companion system is case-insensitive — a referenced companion can lose its 🔒 and be removed

_companions · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/modals/companions.ts:69-74`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/companions.ts:93`, `frontend/static/js/src/companions.ts:45-57`
- **Symptom:** A companion who IS referenced by an expense can show a removable ✕ instead of the 🔒 lock when the expense's `who`/split-key casing differs from the companion's stored name casing, letting the owner remove a companion that has expenses.
- **Root cause:** `referencedNames` is built from raw `e.who` + split keys (companions.ts:69-74) and the lock test is `referencedNames.has(c.name)` (line 93) — an EXACT, case-sensitive Set match. Everywhere else the app treats companion names case-insensitively (findTripCompanion at companions.ts:45-57, and clean_companions case-folds server-side). So 'alice' in an expense vs an 'Alice' companion (e.g. a name typed with different casing into the ManualTab free-text 'who' field, or a CSV upload) won't match the lock, dropping the protection. (Balance math still uses a ghost-roster union so money isn't lost, but the lock — the user-facing guard — is bypassed.)
- **Repro:** 1. On a trip, log an expense and type the payer as 'alice' (lowercase) in the manual 'who' field. 2. Add a companion 'Alice' (capitalized). 3. Open the picker — 'Alice' shows a removable ✕ rather than 🔒, despite being referenced by the expense.
- **Suggested fix:** Lowercase both sides of the lock comparison: build `referencedNames` from `.toLocaleLowerCase()` values and test `referencedNames.has(c.name.toLocaleLowerCase())`, mirroring findTripCompanion / clean_companions.
- **Verifier:** referencedNames is a raw Set of e.who/split keys (modals/companions.ts:69-74) tested with exact `referencedNames.has(c.name)` (line 93) while findTripCompanion/clean_companions are case-insensitive, so a casing mismatch ('alice' vs 'Alice') bypasses the lock — confirmed, but balance math uses a ghost-roster union so no money is lost (only the user-facing guard is skipped), hence P3.

### BUG-076 — [P3][data-loss] Batch import preview filters rows on the FIRST cell being truthy, silently dropping valid rows with an empty first column

_expenses · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.72_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/expenses/BatchUpload.tsx:97`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/upload.ts:323-343`
- **Symptom:** For a custom format whose first spreadsheet column isn't the row's key field (or a Tricount row with an empty Title, or any export with a leading blank column), the entire row is dropped at parse time before it ever reaches the importer — it's not counted in 'Imported' and not listed in 'Skipped'. The user sees fewer rows imported than their file contains with no explanation.
- **Root cause:** The parser keeps a row only if `r.length > 0 && r[0]` (BatchUpload.tsx:97) — i.e. it requires the FIRST cell to be truthy. But which column is meaningful depends on the format/mapping: Tricount keys on column A (Title) but the amount/payer are elsewhere; a custom format may map its required fields to columns B+. A row with a blank first cell but real data in the mapped columns is discarded before runBatchImport's own per-row validation/skip-reporting runs, so it's invisibly lost rather than reported.
- **Repro:** 1. Define a custom format mapping value→B, date→C, etc. (column A unused). 2. Upload a file whose column A is blank for some data rows. 3. Those rows never appear in the preview, aren't imported, and aren't in the skipped list.
- **Suggested fix:** Drop only fully-empty rows: filter on `r.some(cell => cell !== '' && cell != null)` instead of `r[0]`. Let runBatchImport's existing per-field validation + skipped[] reporting handle rows that are genuinely unusable, so nothing is silently discarded.
- **Verifier:** Verified: BatchUpload.tsx:97 keeps a row only if `r.length > 0 && r[0]`, but the meaningful column depends on the format/mapping (a custom format may map required fields to columns B+), so a row with a blank first cell but real mapped data is dropped before runBatchImport's per-row skip-reporting runs — real but minor edge (most rows have a non-empty first cell), P3 stands.

### BUG-077 — [P3][correctness] Import date parser silently discards any date with a 2-digit year, importing common CSV dates as undated 'Global'

_expenses · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.70_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/upload.ts:227-256`
- **Symptom:** Spreadsheet exports that write dates with a 2-digit year (e.g. '12/10/23', '5-3-24') — a very common CSV format — import every such expense with no date, grouped under 'Global'. The user's chronological history, date-range filters, and Insights timeline all silently lose the dates with no warning.
- **Root cause:** parseCellDate requires a 4-digit year token: `const yIdx = parts.findIndex(p => /^\d{4}$/.test(p)); if (yIdx === -1) return '';` (upload.ts:231-232). A 2-digit year never matches, so the function returns '' and the expense is stored with date=''. There's no attempt to expand a 2-digit year (e.g. 20YY) and no per-row signal that the date was dropped, so it looks like the dates were simply absent.
- **Repro:** 1. Tricount CSV with Date column values like '12/10/23'. 2. Import. 3. Every row shows date 'Global' in History; date filters and the Insights timeline omit them.
- **Suggested fix:** Accept 2-digit years by expanding them (e.g. 00-69 → 2000-2069, 70-99 → 1970-1999) when no 4-digit token is present and the other two tokens disambiguate day/month, OR surface dropped-date rows in the import result so the loss is visible rather than silent.
- **Verifier:** Verified: parseCellDate requires a 4-digit year token `parts.findIndex(p => /^\d{4}$/.test(p)); if (yIdx === -1) return ''` (upload.ts:231-232) with no 2-digit-year expansion, so a '12/10/23' string date stores date='' (undated); minor because XLSX typed cells arrive as Date objects (cellDates:true) and only 2-digit-year string CSVs hit this, P3 stands.

### BUG-078 — [P3][correctness] Like count includes blocked users' likes on third-party shares

_feed-social · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.75_

- **Files:** `src/routes/feed.py:163`, `src/routes/blocks.py:148`
- **Symptom:** After A blocks B, the like_count A sees on a third party's share still counts B's like. Less visible than the comment desync (there is no 'expand likes' view), but it violates the block contract that B's engagement should not reach A's surfaces and is the same root cause as the comment-count mismatch.
- **Root cause:** `_attach_engagement_counts` likes query (feed.py:163-168) does `SELECT event_id, COUNT(*) FROM feed_likes ... GROUP BY event_id` with no block filter, and the block sweep (blocks.py:148-162) only removes the blocked user's likes on the blocker's OWN posts, not on third-party posts.
- **Repro:** 1) C shares a public trip. 2) A and B both like it. 3) A blocks B. 4) like_count A sees still includes B's like.
- **Suggested fix:** Exclude blocked-author likes from the like_count COUNT for the viewer (same fix as the comment-count desync).
- **Verifier:** Both the feed like-count (feed.py:163-168) and the toggle endpoint's count (feed.py:1019-1023) are plain COUNT(\*) with no block filter, and the block sweep is scoped to the blocker's own posts (blocks.py:149-162); with no 'who-liked' list shown this is count inflation only, so P3 is correct.

### BUG-079 — [P3][security] Follows have no per-account daily cap — open notification-spam fan-out channel

_feed-social · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `src/routes/follows.py:73`, `src/extensions.py:24`, `src/routes/feed.py:1189`
- **Symptom:** A single account can mass-follow distinct users (60/minute ≈ 86k/day), each first-ever follow generating a 'followed_you' notification on the target's bell. There is no per-account ceiling — the only limit is IP-based and shared across everyone behind a NAT.
- **Root cause:** The limiter is keyed on get_remote_address (extensions.py:24), and follow_user/add_friend have only the per-IP @limiter.limit('60/minute') with NO `user_daily_count` gate. The per-account daily-cap pattern exists for feed_comment (feed.py:1189, 200/day) and trip_create (trips.py:129, 50/day) but was never applied to follows, which the follows.py docstring itself flags as a bell-spam / 'petty follower-count games' risk.
- **Repro:** Script POST /api/follows/<id> across many distinct target ids from one account — each first-time follow drops a notification with no per-account brake.
- **Suggested fix:** Add a per-user daily cap on follow creation (e.g. user_daily_count('follow', user_id) >= N → 429), mirroring the feed_comment gate. Increment only on a NEW follow row so unfollow/refollow toggles don't burn quota.
- **Verifier:** follow_user (follows.py:73) and add_friend (friends.py:187) carry only per-IP @limiter.limit (limiter keyed on get_remote_address, extensions.py:24) with no user_daily_count gate like feed_comment has (feed.py:1189), but the follow notification fires only on the FIRST-EVER follow per pair (follows.py:117-125), so toggling can't re-spam and the residual channel is weak — P3 is appropriate.

### BUG-080 — [P3][bug] Personalized greeting silently always says 'traveler' — server never sends user.firstName

_home · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.90_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/welcomeCard.ts:70-79`, `frontend/static/js/src/bootstrap/auth.ts:58`, `src/routes/auth.py:67-77`, `src/routes/auth.py:185-187`, `src/routes/auth.py:262-264`
- **Symptom:** The 'Hey {name}!' greeting (home.greetingNamed) never shows the user's real first name — it always falls back to 'traveler' (e.g. 'Hey traveler!'). The feature looks implemented but is effectively dead for every user.
- **Root cause:** pickGreeting reads STATE.user.firstName (welcomeCard.ts:70) and falls back to 'traveler' when it's missing. But the server's user payload in EVERY auth endpoint (/api/me at auth.py:67-77, dev-login at 185-187, Google login at 262-264) only sends name, never firstName. The client assigns STATE.user = data.user verbatim (auth.ts:58), so user.firstName is always undefined. The rest of the codebase derives the first name from name (e.g. modals/trip.ts:160 STATE.user.name.split(' ')[0]), so welcomeCard.ts is the odd one out reading a field that's never populated.
- **Repro:** 1. Log in (any account whose name is e.g. 'Maria Silva'). 2. Create a brand-new trip with a country but no days/expenses (so isFresh=true). 3. Reload Home until the random greeting picks the named template — it reads 'Hey traveler!' instead of 'Hey Maria!'.
- **Suggested fix:** Derive the first name from the existing field: const firstName = STATE.user?.name?.split(' ')[0] || 'traveler'; in welcomeCard.ts (mirror modals/trip.ts:160). Alternatively, populate firstName in the server user payload. Confirm the localized 'traveler' fallback word is also translated (home.greetingNamed currently interpolates a hardcoded English 'traveler').
- **Verifier:** Confirmed welcomeCard.ts:70 reads STATE.user.firstName and all three auth payloads send only name, never firstName (auth.py:67-83 /api/me, 185-187 dev-login, 262-272 Google), and STATE.user=data.user is assigned verbatim (auth.ts:58) — the only server firstName fields are on OTHER users in feed.py:523/public.py:635, a different object; downgraded to P3 as it is purely cosmetic and is just 1 of 4 random greeting templates.

### BUG-081 — [P3][correctness] Insights 'Worth today' silently wrong for ~30 live-only currencies (SEK/NOK/DKK/THB/TRY/PLN…) because Model-A vs Model-B hinges on a non-reactive, fire-and-forget FX-overlay race

_insights · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.78_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/utils/presentValue.ts:240`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/presentValue.ts:243`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/currency.ts:88`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/currency.ts:62`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/misc.ts:55`, `frontend/static/js/src/main.ts:106`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/insights/Insights.tsx:563`
- **Symptom:** For a trip in a currency that is NOT one of the 17 baked-in CONVERSION_RATES codes but IS in the live ECB/Frankfurter feed (SEK, NOK, DKK, THB, TRY, PLN, CZK, HUF, AED, ARS-via-feed, etc.), the 'Worth today' figure (and the donut/currency-breakdown in Today mode, and the 'X% pricier/cheaper' readout) can be computed with the wrong model: it grows the frozen euroValue by HOME-country CPI instead of using today's FX × the currency's own CPI. The 'Spent' leg meanwhile uses the correct historical FX for the same currency, so the two legs disagree and the pricier/cheaper delta is spurious. The hero shows a settled (non-'calculating…') but wrong number.
- **Root cause:** The Model-A (has-FX) vs Model-B (no-FX) branch is decided by hasRate(curUp) (presentValue.ts:240). hasRate() only returns true for EUR + CONVERSION_RATES (17 codes) + the live overlay \_liveRates (currency.ts:88-93). The live overlay is populated by refreshFxRates() which is fired fire-and-forget at boot (main.ts:106, `void refreshFxRates()`) and, on success, calls setLiveFxRates() which mutates a MODULE-PRIVATE object and does NOT emit STATE_CHANGED (currency.ts:62-69). The Insights useMemo depends on rateCache/cpiCache/etc. but never on the live overlay, so (a) before the overlay lands hasRate('SEK')=false → Model B is used, and (b) even after it lands the memo does not recompute, and (c) if /api/fx-rates fails outright the wrong model persists for the whole session. The hero gate (heroCalculating, Insights.tsx:563) only waits on the CPI fetch, never on the live overlay, so the wrong figure is shown as final. The historical 'Spent' leg uses rateCache (Frankfurter, which DOES carry SEK), so only the Today leg is wrong → leg mismatch.
- **Repro:** 1) Force /api/fx-rates to fail or be slow (offline at boot, or server 500). 2) Create a trip with a few SEK expenses dated a few years back. 3) Open Insights, switch to 'Worth today'. Observe the SEK contribution is grown by German (EUR) CPI on the euroValue instead of today's SEK rate × Swedish CPI; the 'pricier/cheaper' line reflects this wrong figure. 4) Even with a working endpoint: open Insights immediately on boot before the overlay resolves and stay on the page — the memo does not refresh when the rates arrive.
- **Suggested fix:** Make the FX overlay reactive and gate on it: have setLiveFxRates() (or refreshFxRates) write into STATE and emit(EVENTS.STATE_CHANGED) so Insights recomputes when live rates land, and add a useStore-tracked 'fxReady' flag to heroCalculating in Today mode. Alternatively, decide Model-A/B on whether convertCurrency would return a REAL rate (track which codes came from the live/static tables) rather than the boot-race-sensitive hasRate, and treat 'rate not yet loaded' distinctly from 'currency has no rate'.
- **Verifier:** Mechanics are real: presentValue.ts:240 branches on hasRate(curUp), CONVERSION_RATES (constants.ts:103-121) holds only 17 codes so SEK/NOK/DKK/THB/TRY/PLN are live-overlay-only, setLiveFxRates (currency.ts:62-69) mutates a module-private object with no STATE_CHANGED, and the calc useMemo deps (Insights.tsx:389) + heroCalculating (Insights.tsx:563-565) never reference the overlay — BUT refreshFxRates() fires at app boot (main.ts:106) long before Insights mounts, and the CPI/rateCache fetches that DO retrigger the memo land afterward, so the race self-heals in practice; only an outright /api/fx-rates failure leaves SEK/NOK/etc. permanently on Model B (a bounded, intended home-CPI fallback) for the session, making the residual a narrow methodology mismatch rather than a wildly wrong figure.

### BUG-082 — [P3][correctness] Auto-fill FX suggestion for a PAST year on a non-EUR home mixes at-the-time EUR cost with today's EUR→home rate

_insights · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.62_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/utils/manualRates.ts:186`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/manualRates.ts:188`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/RatesEditor.tsx:420`
- **Symptom:** For a user whose home currency is not EUR, the 'Set automatically from my trips' button (and the auto placeholder) suggests a per-year FX rate that is slightly wrong for past years: it computes the rate the user 'paid' that year by taking the frozen at-the-time euroValue and converting it to home using TODAY's EUR→home rate, then dividing by the original amount. The at-the-time foreign leg is paired with a present-day home leg, the exact cross-leg mismatch the presentValue 'Spent' calc explicitly avoids (its DATA-5 note). The suggested number is off by the home currency's drift vs EUR since that year.
- **Root cause:** computeAutoRate() mode 'fx' computes homeValue = convertFn(euro,'EUR',homeCur) where euro is the at-the-time euroValue but convertFn only knows today's rate (manualRates.ts:186-188). implied = homeValue/value then becomes a year-rate suggestion. There is no historical EUR→home factor applied, so for home≠EUR the implied rate blends two epochs.
- **Repro:** Set home currency to USD. Log a 2018 expense in GBP with a frozen euroValue. Open Settings → Exchange rates, click 'Set automatically from my trips'. The suggested 2018 GBP→USD rate reflects today's USD/EUR, not 2018's, so it is materially off in years where USD moved against EUR.
- **Suggested fix:** Only auto-suggest FX for the CURRENT year on a non-EUR home (mirror the PV4-2 guard already applied for years without expenses), or apply the historical EUR→home rate from rateCache when converting the frozen euroValue for past years. Document that the figure is a best-effort suggestion the user can edit.
- **Verifier:** Real for non-EUR home: manualRates.ts:186 computes homeValue=convertFn(euroValue,'EUR',homeCur) using today's-only EUR→home rate then implied=homeValue/value (line 188), blending the at-the-time foreign value with a present-day home rate; it is gated to blanks-only prefill of years that actually have expenses (RatesEditor.tsx:407,413-420) and is a user-reviewable suggestion, so impact is minor.

### BUG-083 — [P3][correctness] Shortlist 'Add to AM/PM/Eve' ✓ marker and toggle use naive case-insensitive substring matching — false positives for short/substring place names corrupt the wrong plan line

_itinerary · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.78_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:744`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:851-869`
- **Symptom:** A shortlisted place with a short name (e.g. 'Bar', 'Pão', 'Co-op') or whose name is a substring of other text shows a false ✓ on the AM/PM/Eve button whenever any plan line happens to contain that substring. Clicking it then enters 'remove' mode and SPLICES the first plan line that merely contains the substring — deleting an unrelated line the user wrote (e.g. typing 'Barcelona Cathedral' makes the 'Bar' button show ✓, and clicking it removes the 'Barcelona Cathedral' line).
- **Root cause:** Presence is detected with `planVals[time].includes(place.name.toLowerCase())` (line 744) and removal does `lines.findIndex(l => l.toLowerCase().includes(needle))` + splice (lines 862-863). Plain substring matching with no word-boundary or whole-line check; the add format is '- {name}' but the detector matches the bare name anywhere.
- **Repro:** Add a to-do place named 'Bar'. In the day modal's Morning textarea type 'Barcelona Cathedral'. The 'AM' button for 'Bar' shows ✓. Click it: the 'Barcelona Cathedral' line is deleted.
- **Suggested fix:** Match on the exact appended line format (e.g. test for a line equal to or starting with '- {name}' after trim) rather than a bare substring, or store an explicit per-place membership marker instead of inferring it from free text.
- **Verifier:** Presence is `planVals[time].includes(place.name.toLowerCase())` (dayDetailModal.ts:744) and removal is `lines.findIndex(l => l.toLowerCase().includes(needle))`+splice (862-863) with no word-boundary/whole-line check while the add format is '- {name}', so a short name that is a substring of another line false-positives the ✓ and strips/mismatches the wrong line (the code comments even acknowledge the loose substring behavior).

### BUG-084 — [P3][bug] Dropping a day pin on the map doesn't persist to local storage until 'Save pin' — navigating away loses the placed pin

_itinerary · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/handlers.ts:113-119`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/handlers.ts:165-176`
- **Symptom:** After clicking 'Add pin' and clicking the map to drop a location, if the user navigates away (switches trip, changes page) before clicking 'Save pin', the dropped coordinates are lost — the day reverts to unpinned.
- **Root cause:** The armed map-click listener in addDayPin sets day.lat/lon/lng and calls navigate('home', null, true) but does NOT emit('state:changed') (handlers.ts:113-119), so localStorage isn't updated and the server isn't written. Persistence happens only in saveDayPin (which emits + upsertDay). The in-memory mutation survives only until the next full reload/state hydration, after which it's gone. (cancelPinEdit and deleteDayPin both emit; the drop path is the inconsistent one.)
- **Repro:** Click 'Add pin' on a day, click the map to drop a marker, then switch to another trip or reload without clicking 'Save pin' — the pin is gone.
- **Suggested fix:** Either emit('state:changed') in the drop listener so the dropped coords persist locally (treating Save as the server-commit), or auto-call saveDayPin on drop. At minimum persist optimistically so a mid-flow navigation doesn't silently discard the user's placement.
- **Verifier:** addDayPin's map-click listener (handlers.ts:113-119) sets day.lat/lon/lng and calls navigate() but never emit('state:changed'), whereas cancelPinEdit (161), saveDayPin (172) and deleteDayPin (189) all emit — so the dropped coords live only in memory until saveDayPin runs upsertDay, and a reload before saving loses them.

### BUG-085 — [P3][correctness] Imported template to-dos are pre-ticked for AI (forAI:true) — friend's very first AI generation silently includes the creator's places in the prompt

_journey-creator-template · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.50_

- **Files:** `src/routes/templates.py:85-109`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/ai/useAiPlan.ts:296-298`
- **Symptom:** When the friend opens the AI planner on a freshly-imported template trip and generates a plan without visiting the To-do page first, all of the creator's imported places are fed into the LLM prompt as 'must consider' to-dos, because the snapshot preserves forAI:true. The friend may not realize the creator's picks are steering their generation.
- **Root cause:** \_clean_marked_places preserves forAI verbatim (only dayId/timeOfDay are popped, templates.py:85-109). useAiPlan builds the to-do prompt suffix from items where p.forAI && p.forManual (useAiPlan.ts:296-298). Imported items carry the creator's forAI:true, so they auto-participate in the friend's first generation with zero user action. This is mild (the to-do page lets the user untick), and arguably intended, but it is an implicit data hand-off the friend didn't choose.
- **Repro:** Import a template whose places had forAI:true → open AI page → Generate without opening the To-do page → the imported places appear as included to-dos in the generation context.
- **Suggested fix:** Decide intended behavior explicitly. If imported to-dos should start as inert references, reset forAI:false in \_clean_marked_places on import (the user re-opts-in per place). If pre-ticking is intended, leave as-is and document it; this is low severity.
- **Verifier:** \_clean_marked_places preserves forAI/forManual verbatim (templates.py:105-108 pops only dayId/timeOfDay), creator places default to forAI:true && forManual:true (markedPlaces.ts:117,314-315), and runGenerate filters getMarkedPlaces(activeTrip) on exactly `p.forAI && p.forManual` (useAiPlan.ts:297-299) then appends them to the prompt suffix (316), so imported items auto-participate in the friend's first generation with no user action — real but minor/user-correctable, P3 stands.

### BUG-086 — [P3][data-loss] Batch-import companions are never persisted to the server, so the next /api/data poll silently deletes them (orphaning every imported expense's payer/split names)

_journey-money · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.85_
