- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/upload.ts:387-398`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/upload.ts:460-464`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:47-109`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:147-184`
- **Symptom:** A user bulk-imports a Tricount/Splitwise CSV whose 'Paid by' / splits reference travel companions not yet on the trip's roster. The import appears to work: the new people show up in balances and the expenses are saved. ~15s later (on the next background poll) those companions vanish from the trip roster. The imported expenses survive (they were saved per-row) but now reference names that are no longer companions, so they get re-bucketed as 'removed' ghosts in Settlement balances and drop out of the linked-user settle path — the carefully reconstructed who-owes-whom picture silently degrades.
- **Root cause:** runBatchImport mutates activeTrip.companions in local STATE via addTripCompanion(activeTrip, who) and addTripCompanion(activeTrip, name) for split names (upload.ts:390-398), but it NEVER calls upsertTrip(activeTrip). Its only server calls are upsertExpense per row (persists expenses) and a final syncWithServer() (upload.ts:463). syncWithServer() now POSTs an EMPTY body to /api/sync (api.ts:77-81) — it no longer ships trips/companions at all. So the new companions live only in localStorage. On the next pullFromServer, STATE.trips is fully replaced from the server (api.ts:183 `STATE.trips = allTrips.filter(...)`), merging back only the 4 heavy media fields — companions come straight from the server, which never received the import's additions. Net: imported roster additions are wiped on the next poll while their expenses persist, breaking the expense→companion→settlement hand-off.
- **Repro:** 1. Create a trip with only yourself as companion. 2. Expenses → Batch upload a Tricount CSV with rows whose 'Paid by' column = 'Alice', 'Bob' (not yet companions). 3. Import succeeds; open Settlement → Alice/Bob appear with balances. 4. Wait ~15s (or navigate away and back to force a /api/data poll). 5. Alice/Bob are gone from the roster; their expenses now show under a 'removed' ghost in balances and can no longer be settled via the linked-member path.
- **Suggested fix:** After the import loop, persist the trip roster: call upsertTrip(activeTrip) (which ships companions to /api/trips) whenever addTripCompanion added anyone — e.g. track a `rosterChanged` flag in runBatchImport and `if (rosterChanged && activeTrip) void upsertTrip(activeTrip);` before the final emit. Relying on syncWithServer() is wrong because it no longer carries trips.
- **Verifier:** Root cause is real — runBatchImport mutates activeTrip.companions via addTripCompanion (upload.ts:391,396) but never calls upsertTrip, and syncWithServer now POSTs an empty body (api.ts:77-81), so on the next pull STATE.trips is replaced from the server (api.ts:183) and the import's roster additions are gone; BUT the 'orphaning payer/split names' impact is overstated because computeTripBalances/byCurrency rebuild the roster as a UNION of trip.companions AND each expense's persisted who+splits keys (balances.ts:161-170,240-243) and upsertExpense persists who+splits server-side (expenses.py:240-264), so settlements still compute correctly — only the saved chip-panel/Who-Paid roster transiently loses import-only names.

### BUG-087 — [P3][correctness] Batch import splits early rows across a smaller companion roster than later rows, because addTripCompanion grows the roster mid-loop

_journey-money · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.70_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/upload.ts:390-412`
- **Symptom:** When importing a Tricount/Splitwise file where the equal-split default applies (no explicit splits column), rows imported earlier in the file are split across fewer people than rows imported later, because each row's 'Paid by' adds a new companion that only affects subsequent rows. The same trip's expenses end up with inconsistent equal-share denominators, so per-person balances are subtly wrong even before the roster-persistence bug (finding #1) wipes the companions.
- **Root cause:** Inside the parsedRows.forEach loop, runBatchImport first calls addTripCompanion(activeTrip, who) for the current row (upload.ts:390), then computes the equal-split default from getTripCompanionNames(activeTrip) (upload.ts:404-408). Because the roster is mutated incrementally as rows are processed, tripRoster.length grows during the loop: row 1 (only 'Alice' known) splits 100% to Alice; row 5 (after Alice, Bob, Carol seen) splits 33/33/33. The split denominators are not stable across the import, so equal-share expenses don't reflect the final companion set.
- **Repro:** 1. Trip with only yourself. 2. Import a Tricount CSV: row1 Paid by Alice, row2 Paid by Bob, row3 Paid by Carol, all with no splits column. 3. Open Settlement balances → early rows are split across fewer people than later rows; the resulting balances don't match an equal 4-way split of every expense.
- **Suggested fix:** Two-pass the import: first walk all rows to collect every 'who' + split name into the roster, THEN build each row's equal-split default against the complete roster. (And persist the roster once via upsertTrip per finding #1.)
- **Verifier:** Inside parsedRows.forEach (upload.ts:314) each row first calls addTripCompanion(activeTrip, who) (line 391) and then, only for rows with NO explicit splits column in the Tricount/Splitwise branch, computes the equal split from getTripCompanionNames(activeTrip) (lines 404-408) which reflects only companions seen so far, so early rows split across fewer people than later rows; with no pre-pass to seed the full roster (runBatchImport 283-314 confirms none) the claim holds, but severity is P3 — it only affects popular-format imports lacking a per-row splits column, is an intent-mismatch rather than data corruption, and is user-editable afterward.

### BUG-088 — [P3][bug] Autocomplete predictions can render out of order (stale response overwrites newer) — no request-sequence guard

_maps · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.78_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:185`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:210`
- **Symptom:** While typing quickly, the dropdown can briefly show predictions for an earlier query than what's currently in the input (e.g. input says 'paris' but the list shows 'par…' results), because the earlier in-flight request resolved after the later one. Clicking such a stale row searches the wrong place.
- **Root cause:** The 220ms debounce (typingTimer) limits request frequency but does not serialize responses. getPlacePredictions callbacks (line 210) call renderPredictions(preds) with no token/sequence check, so a slower earlier response that lands after a faster later one wins. There is no 'latest request id' comparison and no comparison of the response against the current searchInput.value.
- **Repro:** 1. Throttle network (Slow 3G). 2. Type 'par' then quickly 'paris'. 3. If the 'par' request resolves last, the dropdown shows 'par' predictions under the 'paris' input. Intermittent but reproducible under latency/jitter.
- **Suggested fix:** Add a monotonically increasing request counter captured per getPlacePredictions call; in the callback, ignore the result if its counter !== the latest issued, or if searchInput.value.trim() no longer matches the query that was sent.
- **Verifier:** The 220ms debounce (mapSearch.ts:193) only limits frequency; the getPlacePredictions callback (210-220) calls renderPredictions with no request-id/token and no check against current searchInput.value, so a slower earlier response landing after a faster later one wins — genuine but low-frequency, P3.

### BUG-089 — [P3][security] Media POST does not validate/sanitize item URLs — arbitrary src/url (incl. javascript:) persisted into trip media

_media · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `src/routes/trips.py:719`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/tripMediaModals.ts:953`, `frontend/static/js/src/tripMedia.ts:113`
- **Symptom:** A user (or a crafted client) can store a photo/document whose `src`/`url` is an arbitrary string — `javascript:...`, `data:text/html,...`, or a path into another user's /static/uploads subdir. The link-card click does `window.open(photo.src, '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer')`, and the value is echoed into the DOM; while modern browsers + the global CSP/nosniff blunt most of it, storing unsanitized scheme-bearing URLs in shared trip data is a latent stored-XSS / link-abuse vector that other members also render.
- **Root cause:** `update_trip_media` (trips.py:719-732) validates only that each field is a list and within the 512KB cap — it never validates the items' URL scheme or ownership, unlike the expense path which runs `validate_upload_url` on `receipt_url`. The client `addTripPhoto`/`addTripDocument` (tripMedia.ts:113, :95) store the raw user-typed string with no scheme allowlist. Cross-user /static/uploads exfiltration is separately blocked by serve_upload's membership gate, but javascript:/data: schemes and external-link abuse are not filtered anywhere.
- **Repro:** Open Add photo by link, paste `javascript:alert(document.cookie)` (or a data:text/html URL), save. It persists into trip.photos[].src and is rendered as a link card; clicking opens the scheme.
- **Suggested fix:** Server-side: in `update_trip_media`, validate each item's url/src against an allowlist (http(s) or the app's own /static/uploads/<caller>/ prefix via validate_upload_url) and reject/strip others. Client-side: enforce the same scheme allowlist in addTripPhoto/addTripDocument and refuse javascript:/data:text-html.
- **Verifier:** update_trip_media (trips.py:719-732) checks only list-ness + 512KB cap and never runs validate_upload_url (unlike expenses.py:104), and addTripPhoto/addTripDocument store the raw string (tripMedia.ts:113/95); esc() (dom-helpers.ts:104-112) entity-escapes but does NOT strip the javascript: scheme, so a planted document href="javascript:..." (tripMediaModals.ts:155) is a real but browser-mitigated, click-gated vector (photo background-image url() is quote-escaped, no CSS breakout) -> P3.

### BUG-090 — [P3][correctness] convertCurrency silently falls back to 1:1 for any code missing from both live and static tables, so a stored amount in a now-unsupported currency renders at a fabricated rate

_money-invariant · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/utils/currency.ts:71`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/currency.ts:77`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/currency.ts:119`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/currency.ts:123`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/currency.ts:137`
- **Symptom:** If an expense or budget was stored with a currency that is NOT EUR and is absent from both the live Frankfurter overlay and the static CONVERSION_RATES table (e.g. the live feed drops a code, or a legacy/imported row carries an exotic code), any DISPLAY conversion through convertCurrency treats 1 unit = 1 EUR. A budget 'was 270000 VND' suffix, or a Settle 'primary currency' hint, can show a grossly wrong home figure (270000 displayed as if €270000) with no warning.
- **Root cause:** \_rateFor returns `CONVERSION_RATES[upper] || 1` (currency.ts:77) — the 1.0 fallback is silent. convertCurrency multiplies by this 1:1 rate (currency.ts:119-123), and formatHome (currency.ts:137) and Insights/Settle display callers route through it without first checking hasRate(). The write paths were hardened (expenses C1, settlements S2, budgets IA-10 all gate on get_rate_eur / hasRate), but the DISPLAY-time convertCurrency keeps the legacy 1:1 fallback, so a row that slipped in under the old rules — or whose code later leaves the feed — renders at a fabricated rate. Balance/budget math reads the stored euro_value (safe), but the original-amount and per-currency display hints call convertCurrency directly.
- **Repro:** Seed a budget with originalCurrency='VND', originalAmount=270000 (or any code absent from the static table while the live feed lacks it). The Budgets card 'was' suffix calls formatHome(270000,'VND') → convertCurrency 1:1 → shows ~€270,000.
- **Suggested fix:** Have convertCurrency (or its display-time callers formatHome/Insights/Settle hints) consult hasRate() and, when false for a non-EUR code, render an explicit 'no rate' / raw-currency label instead of silently applying 1:1 — matching the write-path gates so display and storage agree on 'we cannot convert this'.
- **Verifier:** \_rateFor returns CONVERSION_RATES[upper] || 1 (currency.ts:77) — a silent 1.0 fallback that convertCurrency (119-123) and formatHome (137) propagate with no hasRate guard, while the write paths were all hardened (expenses C1, server settlements compute_euro_value/euroValue-required settlements.py:224-229, budgets IA-10 line 64); balance/budget math reads the stored euroValue (safe) and the live per-currency display hint is hasRate-gated (SettlementView.tsx:302), so the only trigger is a row whose code slipped past write-time gates or later left the live feed rendering at 1:1 — a genuine but minor display-only latent edge, matching the reported P3.

### BUG-091 — [P3][bug] clearLocalState resets STATE.notifications but not STATE.notificationsTotalUnread (badge-count state diverges from documented full-reset invariant)

_notifications · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.72_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/api/core.ts:94-156`, `frontend/static/js/src/bootstrap/notifications.ts:41-58`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/profile.ts:79-80`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/core.ts:269-277`
- **Symptom:** clearAuthToken/clearLocalState (the SY7/R2 'wipe all user-scoped STATE on logout' routine) zeroes STATE.notifications but leaves STATE.notificationsTotalUnread at the previous user's value. Because updateNotificationUI prefers notificationsTotalUnread (notifications.ts:47-49), the badge can momentarily reflect the prior user's unread count after a 401-driven session drop before the next poll reconciles.
- **Root cause:** core.ts:118 sets `STATE.notifications = []` (and resets 8 other fields) but never resets notificationsTotalUnread. The parallel explicit-logout path in profile.ts DOES reset it (profile.ts:80), proving the omission is an oversight, not intent. The leak is largely masked because updateUserUI toggles the 'is-signed-out' body class (hiding the bell) when STATE.user is null, and the 401 path emits state:changed → updateUserUI; but the field still carries stale cross-user state that any future code reading it (or a render before the class applies) would surface.
- **Repro:** Hard to see visually due to CSS masking, but reproducible in state: 1. User A (5 unread) triggers a 401 (expired/revoked token) → core.ts:269 calls clearAuthToken → STATE.notifications=[] but notificationsTotalUnread stays 5. 2. Inspect STATE: notificationsTotalUnread === 5 with notifications === [] — an inconsistent pair until the next fetchNotifications overwrites it post-relogin.
- **Suggested fix:** Add `STATE.notificationsTotalUnread = 0;` next to `STATE.notifications = [];` in clearLocalState (core.ts ~line 118) so the badge-count field is reset on every teardown path, matching profile.ts logout.
- **Verifier:** The cited function (actually named clearAuthToken, core.ts:82-157, not clearLocalState) sets STATE.notifications=[] plus 8 other fields at line 118 but never resets notificationsTotalUnread (grep finds zero refs to it in core.ts), while the explicit-logout path profile.ts:79-80 resets both — and the badge prefers notificationsTotalUnread (notifications.ts:47-49); real stale-state leak but largely masked by the is-signed-out body class hiding the bell when STATE.user is null, so P3 (note: the finding mislabels the function name).

### BUG-092 — [P3][correctness] Cover 'SPEND' stat truncates the total instead of rounding (€842.90 shows as €842)

_pdf · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:360`
- **Symptom:** The cover-page SPEND tile rounds the trip total DOWN to the next whole euro by truncation. A trip with €842.90 total spend shows '€842'; €99.99 shows '€99'. It always under-states by up to ~€1, which looks like an off-by-one to a user who knows their total.
- **Root cause:** `stats.append((f"€{tr.num(int(trip_row['total_spend_eur']), 0)}", ...))` (**init**.py:360) casts to `int()` first, which truncates toward zero, THEN formats with 0 decimals. `tr.num(value, 0)` already rounds-to-nearest via Python format spec, so the extra `int()` both is redundant and forces truncation instead of rounding.
- **Repro:** 1. Add expenses totalling €842.90 to a trip. 2. Export the PDF. 3. The cover SPEND tile reads '€842' (should be '€843' rounded, or show the decimals).
- **Suggested fix:** Drop the `int()` and pass the float directly: `tr.num(trip_row['total_spend_eur'], 0)` so it rounds to the nearest euro (or show 2 decimals to match the rest of the money formatting).

### BUG-093 — [P3][data-loss] Switching the FX↔Inflation Personalization tab discards unsaved rate edits with no confirmation

_rates-editor · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.75_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Personalization.tsx:181-182`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/RatesEditor.tsx:127`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/RatesEditor.tsx:276-287`
- **Symptom:** A user fills in several FX cells but hasn't clicked Save, then taps the 'Inflation' pill (or 'Categories'). The FX editor unmounts and all typed edits are lost. Coming back to the FX tab shows the empty/auto state. Only a soft 'Unsaved changes' hint exists; there's no confirm-before-discard guard.
- **Root cause:** Personalization renders the editor conditionally per tab (`{tab === 'fx' ? <RatesEditor mode="fx"/> : null}`), so switching tabs unmounts the component and its local `draft` state. Edits live only in component state until Save (by design, RatesEditor.tsx:24-25), and nothing blocks/preserves them across an unmount.
- **Repro:** 1. Settings → Exchange rates. 2. Type values into 2-3 cells (don't Save). 3. Click the 'Inflation' pill, then back to 'Exchange rates'. 4. The typed values are gone.
- **Suggested fix:** Either persist the draft across tab switches (lift draft state up, or keep both editors mounted via CSS hidden), or add a confirm() / inline 'You have unsaved changes — discard?' guard when leaving a dirty rate tab. At minimum, keep the editor mounted (display:none) so its draft survives.
- **Verifier:** Personalization.tsx:181-182 renders the two editors as separate conditional `{tab===... ? <RatesEditor/> : null}` blocks, so switching tab unmounts the active RatesEditor and its local `draft` state (RatesEditor.tsx:127), which by design only persists on Save — nothing blocks or preserves the unsaved edits across the unmount; minor display-only loss requiring a deliberate tab switch with unsaved edits.

### BUG-094 — [P3][correctness] Importing a well-formed FX file that only contains the home-currency row shows a false 'couldn't read that file' error

_rates-editor · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.70_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/RatesEditor.tsx:483-507`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/RatesEditor.tsx:530-535`
- **Symptom:** In FX mode, if the imported spreadsheet's only currency rows are the user's home currency (e.g. home=EUR and the file has an EUR row), the import reports the red error 'Couldn't read that file — check it has a Currency column and year headers', even though the file was perfectly well-formed. The user is misled into thinking their file is malformed.
- **Root cause:** applyParsedCells skips every cell where `isFx && currency === home` (lines 488, 498) since FX has no home row, so `applied` stays 0. onImportFile treats `applied === 0` as a hard failure and calls setImportError(true) (lines 532-534), conflating 'nothing applicable' with 'unreadable file'.
- **Repro:** 1. Home currency EUR. 2. Settings → Exchange rates. 3. Import a CSV `Currency,2020\nEUR,1`. 4. See the red 'Couldn't read that file…' error despite a valid file.
- **Suggested fix:** Distinguish 'parsed but nothing applicable' from 'unparseable'. If parseRatesGrid returned cells but all were dropped as home-currency FX, show a specific, non-error notice (e.g. 'No applicable rows — the home currency has no exchange rate to set') instead of the generic read error.
- **Verifier:** applyParsedCells skips every isFx && currency===home cell (RatesEditor.tsx:488,498) so applied stays 0, and onImportFile treats applied===0 as a hard failure → setImportError(true) (lines 532-534), conflating 'nothing applicable' with 'unreadable'; genuine but very edge-case since the FX template excludes the home row (rowCurrencies filter, line 98) so a user must hand-craft a home-only file.

### BUG-095 — [P3][correctness] POST /api/settlements does not re-verify the two parties are STILL accepted members at read time, and snapshots names only — a kicked member's fabricated settlement persists in the balance graph

_security · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.50_

- **Files:** `src/routes/settlements.py:231-238`, `src/routes/data.py:1175-1184`
- **Symptom:** create_settlement validates that from/to are accepted members at creation time (lines 235-238) but the settlement row is then permanent. If a member is later removed (remove_trip_member) the settlement still ships in /api/data to all remaining members and still applies to the shared balance graph. Combined with the third-party-recording gap above, a planner can record a settlement involving a member, then remove that member; the row keeps skewing balances with no party left to delete it except the owner.
- **Root cause:** Settlements are immutable post-creation and /api/data (data.py:1178-1184) selects ALL settlements for the trip with no re-check that from_user_id/to_user_id are still members. remove_trip_member (trips.py:1103) deletes the trip_members row but does not sweep or flag the member's settlements.
- **Repro:** Record a settlement for member B, then remove B from the trip. B's settlement still appears in every remaining member's /api/data and still shifts the balance map.
- **Suggested fix:** On member removal, either tombstone/flag settlements where the removed user is a party, or have the balance reducer ignore settlements whose parties are no longer members. Alternatively, gate /api/data settlement inclusion on current membership of both parties.

### BUG-096 — [P3][bug] /api/sync expense and trip_days loops KeyError → uncaught 500 on a bulk payload entry missing `id` or `tripId`

_security · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.78_

- **Files:** `src/routes/data.py:630-714`, `src/routes/data.py:795-838`, `src/routes/data.py:543-545`
- **Symptom:** An authenticated client (legacy, buggy, or curl) that POSTs /api/sync with an entry in `expenses[]` / `trip_days[]` / archived `expenses[]` that omits `id` (or `tripId`) triggers `e['id']` / `e['tripId']` / `d['id']` / `d['tripId']` KeyError → uncaught 500. The top-of-handler duplicate guard only defensively coerces missing ids for `trips`/`archived_trips` (data.py:245-247), not for the expense/day loops, and `_validate_sync_expense` runs AFTER the `e['id']` SELECT.
- **Root cause:** The per-row loops use subscript access (`e['id']`, `e['tripId']`, `d['id']`, `d['tripId']`) instead of `.get()` with a skip/continue, unlike the per-row delta endpoints which validate id presence and return a clean 400. The SEC-2 hardening covered non-dict BODIES but not missing per-row keys inside the bulk arrays.
- **Repro:** POST /api/sync (authenticated) with body {"expenses":[{"value":5,"currency":"EUR","tripId":"t1"}]} (no id) → 500 instead of a clean skip/400. Same with a trip_days entry lacking id/tripId.
- **Suggested fix:** Guard each loop: `if not isinstance(e, dict) or not e.get('id') or not e.get('tripId'): continue` (mirror the partial-sync silent-skip contract the loops already use for permission failures). Same for the day loop.

### BUG-097 — [P3][security] /components design-system gallery is served publicly with no auth in production

_security · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.55_

- **Files:** `src/main.py:1234-1240`
- **Symptom:** The component-preview page (every UI primitive in every state) renders for any anonymous visitor in production. It exposes internal design-system structure / class names and is a non-product surface that shouldn't be reachable on the live site. Low impact (no user data), but it's an unintended public attack/recon surface and dead weight on the prod routing table.
- **Root cause:** components_preview() has no @require_auth and no dev-env gate (unlike the JWT-secret and rate-limit guards which check \_is_dev_env()). It renders templates/components.html unconditionally.
- **Repro:** Hit https://<prod-host>/components while logged out → the full component gallery renders.
- **Suggested fix:** Gate the route behind \_is_dev_env() (404 in prod) or behind @require_auth + an admin check, matching how other dev-only affordances are handled.

### BUG-098 — [P3][correctness] Bulk /api/sync lets a non-owner planner write trips.is_archived — the share/clone gate's source of truth — diverging from the owner-only mirror the dedicated archive route enforces

_sharing · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.70_

- **Files:** `src/routes/data.py:340`, `src/routes/data.py:380`, `src/routes/trips.py:491`, `src/routes/public.py:540`, `src/routes/trips.py:1541`, `src/routes/trips.py:1550`
- **Symptom:** The legacy bulk-sync trips loop writes trips.is_archived for any trip the caller can edit, including a non-owner planner. trips.is_archived is exactly what the public share read (fetch_share_payload, public.py:540) and both clone paths (trips.py:1541/1550) use to decide whether a shared trip is 'archived = stop serving / refuse clone'. So a non-owner can flip the owner's share-availability state: a non-owner archiving their own copy can set trips.is_archived=1 (killing the owner's live share link), and a non-owner with the trip active can write trips.is_archived=0 (re-enabling a share the owner thought was archive-blocked).
- **Root cause:** The dedicated archive_trip/unarchive_trip routes mirror trips.is_archived ONLY when is_trip_owner is true (trips.py:491-497, 581-587). But the bulk /api/sync active-trips ON CONFLICT writes is_archived=excluded.is_archived unconditionally (data.py:340) from the caller's payload value (data.py:380 `1 if t.get('is_archived') else 0`), gated only by editable_trip_ids — which includes non-owner planners. The first-party frontend now sends an empty /api/sync body so this is dormant for current clients, but the endpoint still accepts a crafted {"trips":[{"id":...,"is_archived":0|1}]} payload from any authenticated editor, and the archive source-of-truth (trips.is_archived) used by the share gate is decoupled from the per-member trip_members.is_archived the rest of the app uses.
- **Repro:** As a non-owner planner of trip T (T shared+live by the owner, not archived), POST /api/sync with body {"trips":[{"id":"T","name":"...","country":"...","is_archived":1}]}. trips.is_archived flips to 1 (data.py:340). Now /share/<token> for T returns the 'not available' page and /api/share/<token>/clone returns 410 — the owner's live share link is dead, set by a non-owner.
- **Suggested fix:** Gate the trips.is_archived write in the bulk-sync loop to owner-only, mirroring the dedicated route: only set is_archived from the payload when t['id']'s owner == user_id; otherwise leave the column untouched (write the caller's state to trip_members.is_archived only, which the loop already does at data.py:419-423). Longer term, retire the legacy trips.is_archived column the share/clone gate depends on and compute archive-availability from the owner's trip_members row.
- **Verifier:** The /api/sync UPSERT writes is_archived=excluded.is_archived unconditionally (data.py:340) from the payload (data.py:380) gated only by editable_trip_ids, which batch_editable_trip_ids includes role=='planner' non-owners (helpers.py:291); data.py:307-313 pins isPublic for non-owners but nothing pins is_archived, whereas archive_trip/unarchive_trip only mirror trips.is_archived when is_trip_owner (trips.py:491-497, 581-587), and trips.is_archived is the share gate's source of truth (public.py:540) — dormant because the first-party client sends body {} (api.ts:80) but a crafted payload from any authenticated editor still works.

### BUG-099 — [P3][correctness] cpiCache / rateCache are persisted but not validated or non-finite-healed on load (NaN can reach the inflation factor), unlike the sibling money maps

_state · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.55_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:42`, `frontend/static/js/src/schemas.ts:198`, `frontend/static/js/src/utils/presentValue.ts:45`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/insights/Insights.tsx:824`
- **Symptom:** A corrupt/half-flushed/hand-edited localStorage snapshot with a non-finite value inside cpiCache (e.g. cpiCache.USD['2019']=null/NaN in a non-latest year) flows straight into STATE on load and into makeInflationFactor, which can return NaN for a mid-series gap (valForYear walks down only on null/undefined, and todayVal/base → NaN survives Math.min(MAX, Math.max(0, NaN)) === NaN). That NaN poisons Insights totals/the donut, the same failure class the team explicitly hardened against for the other money maps.
- **Root cause:** validateLoadedState (schemas.ts:198-225) only shape-checks top-level arrays + activeTripId + user; it does not inspect rateCache/cpiCache. loadState() adds explicit non-finite healing loops for STATE.fxOverridesByTrip (state.ts:146-165) and STATE.manualRates (state.ts:170-188) — with a comment that a corrupt override 'could carry NaN/Infinity into the Insights calc and poison every total' — but cpiCache/rateCache, which feed the identical calc, get no equivalent heal. The runtime guards in presentValue.ts cover the override (ovValid, IA-1) and manual (Number.isFinite(manualPct)) branches but not the auto CPI branch, where makeInflationFactor only guards latestVal !== 0, not interior values.
- **Repro:** Set localStorage 'theGreatEscapeState' with a valid-shaped object whose cpiCache.USD has {'2010':100,'2015':null,'2024':140} and an expense in 2015, then load Insights in 'Worth today' mode → the USD expense's todayValue (and the headline total) renders NaN.
- **Suggested fix:** Add a non-finite heal for cpiCache/rateCache in loadState() mirroring the fxOverridesByTrip/manualRates loops (drop any year/key whose value isn't a finite number > 0). Belt-and-braces: in makeInflationFactor's valForYear, treat a non-finite interior value like a gap (walk down) and final-guard `return Number.isFinite(f) ? Math.min(MAX, Math.max(0,f)) : 1`.
- **Verifier:** validateLoadedState (schemas.ts:198-225) shape-checks only the 8 arrays + activeTripId + user and loadState heals fxOverridesByTrip/manualRates for non-finite (state.ts:146-188) but never cpiCache/rateCache, which feed the identical calc via makeInflationFactor(cpiCache[cur]) (Insights.tsx:824/267); the asymmetry is real and makeInflationFactor only guards latestVal!==0 — an Infinity latestVal slips past to a NaN output factor (most interior NaNs are self-healed by `v || latestVal` / `base ?`), so a genuine-but-theoretical hardening gap given these caches come from server fetches, not user input.

### BUG-100 — [P3][correctness] Public template preview counts the internal Trip-Hub anchor as a day (off-by-one 'days planned') and renders it as a ★ row to strangers

_templates · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `src/routes/templates.py:161-180`, `src/routes/templates.py:518-536`, `frontend/templates/template.html:96`, `frontend/templates/template.html:105-111`
- **Symptom:** On the public share page /t/<code>, a 5-day itinerary advertises '6 days planned', and the read-only itinerary list shows an extra leading row rendered as '★ Trip Hub' (the app's internal starting-point anchor) with no plan content. The same inflated dayCount is returned by the JSON preview API. A stranger evaluating whether to copy the template sees a wrong day count and an unexplained internal concept.
- **Root cause:** \_build_template_snapshot selects ALL non-deleted trip_days ORDER BY day_number with no `day_number > 0` filter (templates.py:162-167), so the snapshot's `days` array includes the lazily-created Trip-Hub anchor (dayNumber 0; created client-side in pages/home-mount/handlers.ts:246-260, so it exists for any trip the creator has opened on Home). fetch_template_preview then sets dayCount = len(days) (templates.py:527), counting day 0, and passes day 0 through to template.html, which renders dayNumber==0 as a ★ 'Trip Hub' row (template.html:106-111). The anchor usually has empty plan slots so it shows as a contentless extra row.
- **Repro:** 1) As a creator open a trip on Home (creates the day-0 anchor) and add e.g. 5 numbered days with plans. 2) Publish a template with plans included. 3) Open /t/<code> in a logged-out browser (or GET /api/templates/preview/<code>): the stats chip reads '6 days planned' for a 5-day trip and the itinerary list begins with a ★ Trip Hub row.
- **Suggested fix:** Exclude the anchor from the public view: either add `AND day_number > 0` to the snapshot day query in \_build_template_snapshot, or filter `d.get('dayNumber')` != 0 out of `days`/`dayCount` inside fetch_template_preview (and skip the is_hub branch in template.html). Note instantiation may still want day 0 to seed the new trip's anchor, so filtering in the public-preview layer (fetch_template_preview) is the safest scoped fix; alternatively keep day 0 in the snapshot for instantiation but never count/show it publicly.
- **Verifier:** Confirmed the day-0 'Trip Hub' anchor is a real persisted trip_days row (handlers.ts:246-266 builds dayNumber:0 and calls upsertDay), the snapshot query has no day_number>0 filter (templates.py:162-167) so day 0 is included, dayCount=len(days) counts it (templates.py:527), and template.html:106-111 renders dayNumber==0 as a ★ Trip Hub row with an empty (but truthy) plan dict; this is a purely cosmetic off-by-one count plus a phantom contentless row with no sensitive content and no data/functional impact, so P3 rather than P2.

### BUG-101 — [P3][bug] Day-Detail shortlist add/remove uses case-insensitive name substring matching — collides when one place name contains another

_todo · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.72_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:744`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:851`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:862`
- **Symptom:** If two shortlisted places have names where one is a substring of the other (e.g. 'Park' and 'Park Güell', or 'Café' and 'Café de Flore'), adding the longer one to a slot makes the shorter one's button show a false ✓, and clicking the shorter one's 'remove' strips the LONGER place's line from the textarea.
- **Root cause:** The shortlist toggle and its ✓ indicator detect presence by `textareaValue.toLowerCase().includes(place.name.toLowerCase())` (dayDetailModal.ts:744 for the ✓ marker, :852 for the add/remove decision) and remove the first line matching that substring (:862). A shorter name is a substring of the line written for a longer name, so the membership test and the line-removal both misfire across the two places.
- **Repro:** 1. Add two places named 'Park' and 'Park Güell' to a trip. 2. Open a numbered day, click 'Park Güell → AM'. 3. The 'Park' row's AM button now shows ✓ even though only 'Park Güell' was added. 4. Click 'Park → AM' (now interpreted as remove): it deletes the '- Park Güell' line.
- **Suggested fix:** Anchor the match to a full line / use an exact-line comparison (e.g. compare trimmed lines to `- ${name}` rather than substring includes), or tag inserted lines with the placeId in a data structure rather than re-deriving membership from free text.

### BUG-102 — [P3][bug] No cap on trip date range → unbounded day scaffolding; days beyond 999 silently rejected by the server

_trips · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/utils/dateRangePicker.ts:89-101`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/_shared.ts:104-127`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:214-229`, `src/routes/days.py:72-73`
- **Symptom:** A user (or a fat-finger on the calendar) who picks a very wide date range (e.g. several years) creates thousands of itinerary days at once. The browser fires thousands of upsertDay POSTs, the day-add hammers the 120/min rate limit, and every day numbered >999 is rejected by the server with a 400 that is never surfaced — so the trip ends up with a few hundred local days that don’t all persist, plus a request storm.
- **Root cause:** mountDateRangePicker configures flatpickr in range mode with NO maxDate and no max-span (dateRangePicker.ts:89-101). \_scaffoldTripDays loops day-by-day from start to end with no upper bound (\_shared.ts:109). The create handler then does Promise.all(scaffolded.map(upsertDay)) (trip.ts:229) with no batching and no error inspection. Server-side upsert_day rejects dayNumber>999 with HTTP 400 (days.py:72-73), but upsertDay’s {ok:false} is ignored, so days 1000..N silently fail while 1..999 persist. The local STATE keeps all N days, diverging from the server.
- **Repro:** 1. New Trip modal, pick destination, open the calendar, select a start and an end ~3 years apart. 2. Submit. 3. Observe a flood of POST /api/days; check the network tab for 400s on day_number>999. 4. The trip has hundreds/thousands of local days but the server stores at most ~999.
- **Suggested fix:** Set a sane maxDate / max-span on the flatpickr range (e.g. cap a trip at ~365 or a few-hundred days) and/or validate the span in \_wireDateRangeValidation with a clear inline error. Also clamp \_scaffoldTripDays to a max count and surface a toast if the range is too long. Align the client cap with the server’s 999 limit.
- **Verifier:** Verified flatpickr is configured with no maxDate/max-span (dateRangePicker.ts:89-101), \_scaffoldTripDays loops unbounded (\_shared.ts:109), Promise.all(scaffolded.map(upsertDay)) ignores each {ok:false} (trip.ts:229), and upsert_day returns 400 for dayNumber>999 (days.py:72-73) so days 1000+ silently fail while local STATE keeps them — real divergence but only triggered by an extreme >999-day (2.7yr) range, so P3.

### BUG-103 — [P3][bug] Maps-unavailable country fallback creates the Day-0 anchor at lat/lng 0,0 (Gulf of Guinea)

_trips · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.74_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/modals/_shared.ts:216-218`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:179-195`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/handlers.ts:240-266`
- **Symptom:** When Google Maps fails to load (ad-blocker, billing/quota, regional block) and the user creates a trip via the country-select fallback, the trip is saved with lat=0,lng=0. When they open the trip home, the auto-created Day-0 'Trip Hub' anchor is pinned at coordinates (0,0) — the middle of the ocean off West Africa — so the map and all anchor-based POI searches center on the wrong place.
- **Root cause:** The Maps-down fallback in \_wirePlacePicker builds the picked place with lat:0,lng:0 (and viewport:null) because it only resolves a country code, not coordinates (\_shared.ts:217-218). The create modal copies these straight onto the trip (trip.ts:184-185). The lazy Day-0 creator gates only on `typeof activeTrip.lat === 'number'` (handlers.ts:243-244) — and 0 IS a number — so it creates the anchor day with lat:0,lng:0 (handlers.ts:252-253). Nothing treats (0,0) as 'no pin yet' on the anchor path (todoMarkers.ts:181 special-cases 0,0 for markers, but the anchor day creation does not).
- **Repro:** 1. Block Google Maps (e.g. disable network for maps.googleapis.com / use an ad-blocker). 2. Open New Trip; the country <select> fallback appears. 3. Type a name, pick a country, Create. 4. Open the trip home → the map and the Trip Hub anchor pin sit at (0,0) in the ocean.
- **Suggested fix:** Treat (0,0)/null-viewport as 'no coordinates' when deciding whether to create the Day-0 anchor (skip creation, or create it without a pin so it renders the 'needs a pin' state). Gate handlers.ts on real coords: `Number.isFinite(lat) && Number.isFinite(lng) && !(lat===0&&lng===0)`.
- **Verifier:** The Maps-down fallback builds the picked place with lat:0,lng:0 (\_shared.ts:218), the create modal copies these onto the trip (trip.ts:184-185), and the lazy Day-0 creator gates only on typeof activeTrip.lat==='number' (handlers.ts:243-244) — 0 IS a number — so it creates the anchor at 0,0 (handlers.ts:252-253) which todoMarkers.ts:181 treats as 'no pin' only for to-do markers not the anchor; real but cosmetic and only when Maps fails to load, so P3.

### BUG-104 — [P3][bug] Editing trip dates with all-undated existing days silently no-ops the date change

_trips · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.62_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:518-549`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:527-535`
- **Symptom:** A trip that has numbered days with no dates (e.g. created without a range, then days added manually without dates) cannot get its dates applied via Edit Trip — the user picks a start/end range, saves, and the days remain undated with no feedback.
- **Root cause:** In the edit-dates branch, oldFirst/oldLast are parsed from numberedDays[0].date / [last].date (trip.ts:527-528). When those dates are empty, parseUTC('') returns null, so startChanged and endChanged (trip.ts:532-535) are both false (they require oldFirst/oldLast to be non-null). The rebase (line 539) and extend/shorten (line 565) blocks are gated on startChanged/endChanged, so nothing runs — the picked dates are written only to trip.dateFrom/dateTo (finalizeAndClose) but never propagated to the day rows. The 'numberedDays.length === 0' scaffold path (line 518) doesn’t apply because numbered days exist (just dateless).
- **Repro:** 1. Create a trip with no dates. 2. Add a couple of days manually (no dates). 3. Open Edit Trip, pick a date range, Save. 4. The days stay undated; only trip-level dateFrom/dateTo change.
- **Suggested fix:** When numbered days exist but are undated, treat it like the scaffold/assign-fresh case: assign date = start + (dayNumber-1) for each numbered day (the same arithmetic the rebase uses), independent of startChanged/endChanged.
- **Verifier:** Verified oldFirst/oldLast parse numberedDays[0].date/[last].date (trip.ts:527-528) which yield null for empty dates, making startChanged/endChanged both falsy (trip.ts:532-535, they require non-null old dates), so the rebase (539) and extend/shorten (565) blocks are skipped and the new dates land only on trip.dateFrom/dateTo (601-602) never on the day rows; the numberedDays.length===0 scaffold path (518) doesn't apply since dateless numbered days exist — real but narrow edge (existing numbered days all blank-dated), so P3.

---

# Part B — Design, UX, accessibility, i18n & performance

## P1 (4)

### DSGN-001 — [P1][a11y] New-Trip modal: 'Trip name', 'Destination' & template-code inputs have no programmatic label (screen reader announces blank fields)

_a11y · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.95_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:41`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:48`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:49`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:52`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:53`
- **Symptom:** A screen-reader user opening 'New Trip' hears the name and destination fields as 'edit text, blank' with no field name. The template-code input has no label at all (placeholder only). They cannot tell which box is which.
- **Root cause:** The `<label class="form-label">` elements for trip name (line 48) and destination (line 52) carry NO `for`/`htmlFor` attribute and do not wrap the input, so there is no programmatic association; the inputs (#tripName, #tripPlaceInput) also have no `aria-label`. The template-code `<input id="templateCodeInput">` (line 41) has only a placeholder. By contrast the date label on line 62 correctly uses `for="tripDateRange"`, so the pattern was known but not applied to the text inputs. The route-level axe gate (tests/e2e/a11y.spec.js) never opens this modal, so the violation is uncaught.
- **Repro:** Open the app with VoiceOver/NVDA on, click 'New Trip', Tab into the first field. It is announced with no name. (Or run axe-core against the open modal DOM — `label` rule fails on #tripName, #tripPlaceInput, #templateCodeInput.)
- **Suggested fix:** Add `for="tripName"` / `for="tripPlaceInput"` to the existing labels (or wrap the inputs), and give #templateCodeInput an `aria-label` (e.g. t('modals.tmplPlaceholder')). Mirror the already-correct date-label pattern.

### DSGN-002 — [P1][a11y] Edit-Trip modal: 'Adventure name' & 'Destination' inputs have unassociated labels (same label gap as New-Trip)

_a11y · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.95_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:253`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:254`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:257`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:258`
- **Symptom:** Editing a trip, the name and destination fields are announced as nameless edit boxes to screen-reader users; the cover-photo file input label (line 277) is likewise unassociated.
- **Root cause:** `<label class="form-label">` on lines 253, 257 (and 277) have no `for` and don't wrap their inputs (#editTripName, #editTripPlaceInput, #editTripCoverInput); inputs carry no `aria-label`. Only the date label (line 264) uses `for=`. WCAG 1.3.1 / 4.1.2 (label / button-name) fail. Uncaught because the route-only axe gate never opens this modal.
- **Repro:** Open a trip → Edit, Tab through fields with a screen reader; name + destination announce with no label.
- **Suggested fix:** Add `for="editTripName"`, `for="editTripPlaceInput"` to the labels (and an `aria-label` or `for` for the cover-photo control).

### DSGN-003 — [P1][a11y] Add-Day modal: 'Where' and 'Date' inputs have labels with no `for` association

_a11y · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.95_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/modals/day.ts:56`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/day.ts:57`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/day.ts:60`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/day.ts:61`
- **Symptom:** When adding a day to a trip, the 'Where' text field and the 'Date' field are announced to assistive tech without their visible label text.
- **Root cause:** `<label class="form-label text-black/50">` on lines 56 and 60 have no `for`; the inputs (#dayName line 57, #dayDate line 61) have ids but no matching label association and no `aria-label`. The inputs already carry ids, so the fix is a one-line `for=` add on each label. Not covered by the route-only axe gate (modal isn't opened during the scan).
- **Repro:** Open a trip → add a day; Tab into 'Where'/'Date' with a screen reader — fields announce nameless.
- **Suggested fix:** Add `for="dayName"` and `for="dayDate"` to the two labels.

### DSGN-004 — [P1][i18n] Day-Journaling modal is 100% hardcoded English (title, prompt, placeholder, buttons, toast) — no i18n at all

_i18n · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.99_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/journalingModal.ts:31`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/journalingModal.ts:32`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/journalingModal.ts:33`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/journalingModal.ts:35`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/journalingModal.ts:36`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/journalingModal.ts:45`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/TripBody.tsx:307`
- **Symptom:** An ES/FR/PT user who opens a day's journaling editor sees the entire modal in English: heading 'Day N Journaling', subtitle 'Capture your memories and stories from {place}', textarea placeholder 'What happened today? How did you feel?', buttons 'Save Story' / 'Close', and the save toast 'Memories saved!'. Every other modal in the app is localized, so this one sticks out badly.
- **Root cause:** journalingModal.ts never imports `t` and emits raw English literals in its innerHTML and showLiquidAlert call. It is the only home-modal that was never migrated to i18n (dayDetailModal.ts has ~40 t() calls, tripMediaModals.ts ~64, tripChecklistModal.ts is fully localized). No locale keys exist for any of these strings (grep for 'Save Story'/'Memories saved'/'Capture your memories' in en.ts returns nothing). It is reachably wired from TripBody.tsx:305-307 via the `.day-journaling-btn` delegate.
- **Repro:** 1. Set language to Español/Français/Português in Settings. 2. Open a trip on Home, open a day. 3. Click the '✍️ Journaling' (Diario/Journal/Diário) button. 4. Observe the modal heading, subtitle, textarea placeholder, both buttons, and the post-save toast are all in English.
- **Suggested fix:** Add a `journalingModal` (or reuse a `journal.*`) key group to en/es/fr/pt with: title (with {n}/{name} slots), subtitle, placeholder, saveBtn, closeBtn, savedToast. Import { t } in journalingModal.ts and replace every literal; replace showLiquidAlert('Memories saved!') with t(...).

## P2 (19)

### DSGN-005 — [P2][a11y] Home map search input has no accessible name (placeholder is not a label)

_a11y · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/MapSearchBar.tsx:43`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/MapSearchBar.tsx:51`
- **Symptom:** Screen-reader users reach the map search box and hear only 'edit text' (or the placeholder, which is not reliably exposed as a name); there is no persistent label describing what the field searches.
- **Root cause:** `<input id="homeMapSearchInput" type="text" ... placeholder={t('home.searchMapPlaceholder')}>` has no `aria-label` and no associated `<label>`. Placeholder text is not an accessible name (WCAG 4.1.2 / 1.3.1). The adjacent magnifier SVG is `aria-hidden`. The route axe gate scans #home but MapSearchBar renders only inside TripView (requires a seeded trip), so a trip-less fresh-app scan won't flag it.
- **Repro:** On a trip's home view, navigate to the search field with a screen reader — no field name. axe `label` rule fails on #homeMapSearchInput when a trip is present.
- **Suggested fix:** Add `aria-label={t('home.searchMapPlaceholder')}` (or a visually-hidden `<label htmlFor="homeMapSearchInput">`) to the input.

### DSGN-006 — [P2][a11y] Map-search results dropdown is not announced (no aria-live / combobox semantics) and offers no arrow-key navigation

_a11y · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:102`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:105`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:119`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/MapSearchBar.tsx:68`
- **Symptom:** A screen-reader user typing in the map search gets no announcement that predictions appeared or that there were 'No matches.'; the input is not exposed as a combobox. Keyboard users cannot arrow-down through results (only Tab to each button), and the input has no aria linkage to the active option.
- **Root cause:** `#homeMapSearchResults` (MapSearchBar.tsx:68) is a plain `<div>` with no `role="listbox"`/`aria-live`; mapSearch.ts populates it via `resultsEl.innerHTML` (lines 105, 109) with rows rendered as bare `<button class="map-search-row">` (line 119-128) — no `role="option"`, no `aria-activedescendant`, no aria-expanded on the input, and the input has no keydown handler for ArrowUp/Down/Enter (only an `input` listener + a results-container click handler at line 224). The 'No matches.' message (line 105) is therefore silent to assistive tech.
- **Repro:** Type 'paris' in the map search with a screen reader running — no result count/announcement; press ArrowDown — nothing happens (must Tab repeatedly).
- **Suggested fix:** Implement the ARIA combobox pattern: `role="combobox"` + `aria-expanded` + `aria-controls` on the input, `role="listbox"` on the results div with `aria-live="polite"` (or a separate polite status region for the count), `role="option"` on each row, and ArrowUp/Down/Enter key handling driving `aria-activedescendant`.

### DSGN-007 — [P2][a11y] Day-modal shortlist AM/PM/Eve toggle buttons: no aria-pressed and their labels are overwritten with hardcoded English

_a11y · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:118`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:747`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:748`
- **Symptom:** These buttons toggle a place into/out of a time slot, but a screen reader never announces their pressed/unpressed state — only a changing `title`. After the first interaction their visible labels are also rewritten to English literals ('🌅 AM', '☀️ PM', '🌙 Eve'), so a French/Spanish/Portuguese user sees the localized label flip to English mid-session.
- **Root cause:** The buttons are rendered with `title` only (line 118-123) and no `aria-pressed`, even though they are stateful toggles (the title flips between add/remove). `refreshShortlistButtons()` then sets `btn.textContent = isThere ? '✓ ' + label : label` where `label = time === 'morning' ? '🌅 AM' : ...` (lines 747-748) — hardcoded English, ignoring the localized `_slotLabel`/`t()` strings used elsewhere in the same modal. So the toggle state is invisible to AT, and the i18n'd glyph+label regresses to English on refresh.
- **Repro:** Open a numbered day's detail modal, click an AM button — with a screen reader the press state isn't announced; in a non-English locale the button text changes to '✓ 🌅 AM'.
- **Suggested fix:** Add `aria-pressed` to each shortlist add button and toggle it in refreshShortlistButtons(); build the visible label from the existing localized `_slotLabel[time]` (or a t() key) instead of the hardcoded `🌅 AM`/`☀️ PM`/`🌙 Eve` literals.

### DSGN-008 — [P2][design-ux] A saved BYO Gemini key permanently disables the shared host-pool fallback — a user with an exhausted personal key is stuck with no way to generate

_ai · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `src/routes/integrations.py:662-677`, `src/routes/integrations.py:809-885`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/ai/useAiPlan.ts:361`
- **Symptom:** Once a user pastes a valid-shape personal Gemini key in Settings/the BYO panel, EVERY generation uses only that key and never the shared host pool — even when the user's personal key is rate-limited/quota-exhausted. The generation fails with a quota/bad-key error whose hint tells them to 'add your own Gemini API key' (which they already did), and there is no fallback to the host pool that other users get for free. The only escape is to manually clear their saved key.
- **Root cause:** runGenerate always sends `gemini_key: (STATE.geminiApiKey || '').trim()` on every request (useAiPlan.ts:361). Server-side, if the key matches the shape regex, using_byo=true and `keys_to_try = [(0, user_key)]` ONLY (integrations.py:673-677) — the else-branch that builds the host pool is skipped. On a quota error from the BYO key, slot 0 is exempt from cooldown and the loop simply exhausts with no host-pool attempt (integrations.py:871-873). There is no 'fall back to host pool if BYO fails' path.
- **Repro:** 1) Save a real but quota-exhausted personal Gemini key. 2) Generate. 3) Get a quota/'bad key' error. 4) Note that despite the shared usage bar showing available host keys, generation never tries them; the only fix is deleting the saved key.
- **Suggested fix:** On a BYO-key quota/auth failure, fall through to the host pool (append \_available_host_keys() after the BYO slot in keys_to_try, or retry on the pool when the BYO attempt returns a quota error), subject to the per-user daily cap. At minimum, surface a distinct error + one-click 'use the shared pool instead' that omits gemini_key for the retry.
- **Verifier:** runGenerate always sends the user's key (useAiPlan.ts:361); when it matches the shape regex using_byo=true and keys_to_try=[(0,user_key)] ONLY, skipping the \_available_host_keys() else-branch (integrations.py:673-677), and on a quota error slot 0 is exempt from cooldown but the loop simply breaks/exhausts with result_text empty (integrations.py:872-887) — there is no fall-back-to-host-pool path, so an exhausted BYO key dead-ends (recoverable only by clearing the key in Settings).

### DSGN-009 — [P2][i18n] Settings → Sessions panel is entirely hardcoded English (no t() calls) — es/fr/pt users see an untranslated device-management screen

_auth · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.95_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Sessions.tsx:92-94`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Sessions.tsx:96-98`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Sessions.tsx:118-133`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Sessions.tsx:168-169`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Sessions.tsx:179-201`
- **Symptom:** A user with the app in Spanish, French, or Portuguese opens Settings → Sessions and sees English: the 'Active sessions' heading, the 'Devices currently signed in… Revoke any you don't recognise.' body, 'This device', 'No active sessions found.', 'Last active … · Signed in …', the 'Sign out'/'Revoke' buttons, and the entire revoke confirmation modal ('Sign out here?', 'This will sign you out on this device…', "Sign out the … device? It'll be signed out within ~15 seconds…").
- **Root cause:** Sessions.tsx self-documents the gap at lines 118-120 ('keys for these strings can be added to the locale tables once the SessionsView ships — for now we hard-code English'). All visible strings are string literals rather than t(...) lookups, and no corresponding keys exist in locales/{en,es,fr,pt}.ts. The relative-time helper \_formatRelativeTime DOES use the i18n table (feed.relTime\*), which makes the surrounding hardcoded strings inconsistent.
- **Repro:** 1. Set language to Español/Français/Português (Settings → General, or via a browser-locale account). 2. Open Settings → Sessions. 3. All labels, the empty/loading states, and the revoke confirmation dialog render in English.
- **Suggested fix:** Add settings.sessions\* keys (title, body, thisDevice, none, loading, lastActive, signedIn, revoke, signOut, and the confirm-modal titles/messages with the {device} interpolation) to all four locale tables and replace the literals in Sessions.tsx with t() calls, matching the pattern already used by \_formatRelativeTime.
- **Verifier:** Sessions.tsx hard-codes 'Active sessions' (123), 'Devices currently signed in...' (124-126), 'Loading…' (129), 'No active sessions found.' (131-132), 'This device' (168), 'Last active...Signed in' (179-180), 'Sign out'/'Revoke' (200) and the modal copy (92-98) as string literals with no t() lookups, and the comment at 118-120 explicitly self-documents the gap; only \_formatRelativeTime routes through t().

### DSGN-010 — [P2][inconsistency] Collections album covers are gradient placeholders for any trip not opened this session (photos never prefetched for the list)

_collections · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections-mount/helpers.ts:163`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections-mount/Collections.tsx:745`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:178`, `frontend/static/js/src/api.ts:317`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections.ts:56`
- **Symptom:** The 'fanned photo stack' album covers show generic colored-gradient tiles instead of trip photos for the typical user. Photos only appear for albums whose trips either have an explicitly-uploaded coverUrl OR were opened (and thus media-hydrated) earlier this session / persisted to localStorage in a prior session. On a fresh login or a new device, every album is gradient even when the trips are full of photos.
- **Root cause:** tripCover() (helpers.ts:163-170) falls back coverUrl → trip.photos[0] → day.photos[0]. But /api/data deliberately ships the four heavy media fields empty; api.ts:178 cold-defaults trip.photos=[] for any trip not yet hydrated. fetchTripMedia() is only ever called for the active trip (api.ts:317), on trip-switch (bootstrap/trip-controls.ts:75), and when opening an archived-trip detail (collections.ts:56). It is NEVER called for the Collections list/overview render, so trip.photos is empty there for un-opened trips. Additionally, photos are written to the TRIP-level trip.photos[] array (addTripPhoto with a dayId), not the legacy trip_days.photos column, so tripCover()'s day.photos[0] fallback (helpers.ts:166-167) is also empty for modern trips. Template-instantiated trips have no coverUrl by design (src/routes/templates.py:257-258), so they are always gradient.
- **Repro:** 1. Have an archived trip with photos but no explicitly-set cover image. 2. Log in fresh (or clear localStorage) and go to Collections with 'Group by continent/year'. 3. Observe the album stack renders gradient tiles, not the trip's photos. 4. Open the trip's detail once, return to Collections — now its cover appears (media got hydrated + persisted).
- **Suggested fix:** Either (a) prefetch media (or a lightweight cover-thumb) for the visible archived trips when the Collections page mounts — e.g. fire fetchTripMedia for the first cover of each album, ideally behind an IntersectionObserver to bound the fan-out; or (b) have the server derive and ship a cover thumbnail in /api/data (e.g. cover_url falls back to first photo) so the album overview has a real image without hydrating full media; or (c) document that albums show photos only after a cover is set / the trip is opened, and lean on the gradient as the intended default.

### DSGN-011 — [P2][design-ux] ArchivedTripDetail shows owner-only Restore + privacy controls on foreign/active trips (dead button + select that persists nothing)

_collections · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections/ArchivedTripDetail.tsx:272`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections/ArchivedTripDetail.tsx:293`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections/handlers.ts:36`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections/handlers.ts:60`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections.ts:42`
- **Symptom:** When a user opens someone else's shared trip (or their own still-active trip) from the Feed or Footprint map, the detail hero renders a 'Restore' button and a privacy <select> (Private / Public-plan / Public-all) as if they own it. Clicking Restore does nothing (silent no-op). Changing the privacy dropdown visibly switches the displayed option but persists nothing — the user believes they changed a trip's visibility when they didn't.
- **Root cause:** ArchivedTripDetail.tsx has no ownership gate — it always renders the Restore button (line 272) and the privacy select (lines 293-303). For foreign trips fetched via /api/public-trip (collections.ts:42 slow path) and for the user's own active trips (fast path), restoreTrip() (handlers.ts:60-62) and toggleTripPrivacy() (handlers.ts:36-37) both look the trip up in STATE.archivedTrips/STATE.trips and early-return when not found, so they no-op. The privacy <select> is uncontrolled (defaultValue), so its displayed value changes on the user's pick even though nothing persisted. The public-trip endpoint already returns ownerId on the trip (src/routes/public.py:185), so an ownership check is feasible.
- **Repro:** 1. As user B, view user A's public archived trip from the Feed. 2. See the 'Restore' pill and the visibility dropdown in the hero. 3. Click Restore → nothing happens. 4. Change the visibility dropdown → it visually changes but no request persists and A's trip is unaffected.
- **Suggested fix:** Gate the Restore button + privacy select (and arguably keep Clone, which is a legit cross-user action) on ownership: render them only when trip.ownerId === STATE.user?.id (or when the trip is found in STATE.archivedTrips). For non-owned trips, hide owner-only controls and keep the page read-only (Back / Share-to-feed-of-own / Clone as appropriate).

### DSGN-012 — [P2][i18n] Day-pin map toasts ('Click on the map…', 'Location saved!', 'Day deleted') are hardcoded English

_i18n · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.97_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/handlers.ts:111`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/handlers.ts:174`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/handlers.ts:321`
- **Symptom:** During a core itinerary action — placing, saving, or deleting a day's map pin — non-English users get English toasts: 'Click on the map to set the location for this day!', 'Location saved!', and 'Day deleted'.
- **Root cause:** handlers.ts imports `t` (line 28) and uses it elsewhere, but these three showLiquidAlert() calls pass bare English string literals. No locale keys exist for them (grep for 'Location saved'/'Click on the map'/'Day deleted' in en.ts returns nothing).
- **Repro:** 1. Switch language to fr/es/pt. 2. On Home with a trip, click 'add pin' on a day → English toast 'Click on the map…'. 3. Click the map then save → 'Location saved!'. 4. Delete a day → 'Day deleted'.
- **Suggested fix:** Add keys (e.g. errors.dayPinClickMap / dayPinSaved / dayDeleted) to all four locales and route these three toasts through t().

### DSGN-013 — [P2][i18n] PDF export modal: 'Expenses', 'Settle up', 'Photos' option labels + descriptions hardcoded in English (acknowledged shortcut)

_i18n · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.98_

A FR/ES/PT user sees a mixed-language modal.
- **Root cause:** Deliberate shortcut documented in-code at modals/pdf.ts:74-77 ('The modal labels are English literals because the brief forbids touching the locale files; the PDF CONTENT is localised server-side'). The renderPdfOption() calls at lines 78-83 pass raw English strings instead of t(). The localized PDF body does not cover this client-side modal UI.

### DSGN-014 — [P2][i18n] Trip-picker shows hardcoded English 'No Active Trips' in navbar/sidebar when user has no trips

_i18n · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.95_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/bootstrap/trip-controls.ts:45`, `frontend/templates/index.html:513`, `frontend/templates/index.html:543`
- **Symptom:** When a user has zero active trips (brand-new account, or after completing/deleting all trips), the always-visible trip-picker dropdown reads 'No Active Trips' in English for every locale. The static fallback placeholder 'Select a Trip...' in index.html is likewise English.
- **Root cause:** updateTripSelector() runs on every state:changed and overwrites the select's innerHTML with `'<option value="">No Active Trips</option>'` (trip-controls.ts:45) — a hardcoded literal, so even a data-i18n attribute on the static option would be clobbered. The module imports `t` (used at line 93+) but not for this string; no key exists for it. The index.html `<option>Select a Trip...</option>` (lines 513/543) also has no data-i18n-key.
- **Repro:** 1. Switch language to fr/es/pt. 2. Be a new user, or complete/delete all trips so STATE.trips is empty. 3. Open the navbar/sidebar trip dropdown → 'No Active Trips' shown in English.
- **Suggested fix:** Add nav.noActiveTrips (and nav.selectATrip) to all four locales; use t() at trip-controls.ts:45 and replace the static index.html option text.
