### DSGN-059 — [P3][i18n] Map InfoWindows + search dropdown are hardcoded English — every place bubble and the search UI ignore the active locale

_maps · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.90_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/HeroMap.tsx:288`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/HeroMap.tsx:302`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:50`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:105`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:151`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/MapSearchBar.tsx:57`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayMarkers.ts:94`
- **Symptom:** A Portuguese, Spanish, or French user sees English throughout the map surface: '📋 Add to to-do list' / '✓ On your to-do list', 'View on Google Maps →' (both POI and to-do bubbles), 'No matches.', 'Search result', the 'On your to-do list' pill, the clear-button title 'Clear', and 'Day N' / '⭐ Trip Hub' headers in day-pin bubbles. The rest of the app (placeholder, pill labels) is localized, so this is a visible inconsistency on a core surface.
- **Root cause:** These strings are written as literal English in the imperative innerHTML builders (HeroMap.tsx buildInfoWindowHtml, mapSearch.ts renderPredictions/\_FALLBACK_CAT.label, todoMarkers.ts openTodoInfoWindow, dayMarkers.ts openDayPinInfoWindow) and in MapSearchBar.tsx's static JSX, rather than going through t(). The surrounding surface (e.g. home.searchMapPlaceholder, poiTooltips.\*) IS localized, confirming this is an oversight not a deliberate degraded path.
- **Repro:** 1. Switch app language to Português/Español/Français. 2. Open a trip on Home, turn on a POI pill, click a pin — bubble shows 'Add to to-do list' / 'View on Google Maps →' in English. 3. Type a query in the map search and select nothing matching — 'No matches.' is English. 4. Click a day pin — header reads 'Day 2' in English.
- **Suggested fix:** Route all of these through t() with new keys (e.g. map.addToTodo, map.onTodo, map.viewOnGoogleMaps, map.noMatches, map.searchResult, map.clear, map.tripHub, map.dayN). Add the keys to en/es/fr/pt locale files. The bubbles already re-build on locale-independent events, so reading t() at build time is sufficient.
- **Verifier:** Literal English confirmed in buildInfoWindowHtml ('View on Google Maps →', to-do button text, HeroMap.tsx:288,302), mapSearch.ts 'No matches.' (105) + \_FALLBACK_CAT.label 'Search result' (50), todoMarkers.ts (151,157), dayMarkers.ts 'Trip Hub'/'Day N' (94-96), and MapSearchBar.tsx Clear title/aria (57-58), while the same surface uses t() for the placeholder (51) and poiTooltips — real but cosmetic, P3 not P2.

### DSGN-060 — [P3][design-ux] Selecting a search result that fails getDetails is a silent dead-end — no marker, no error, dropdown already closed

_maps · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:173`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:224`
- **Symptom:** User clicks a search suggestion and nothing happens: no pin drops, no info bubble, no error toast. The dropdown has already closed and the input shows the place name, so the user is left thinking the app froze. Happens on OVER_QUERY_LIMIT, NOT_FOUND, REQUEST_DENIED, a transient network error, or quota exhaustion.
- **Root cause:** fetchDetails (mapSearch.ts:175-182) calls svc.getDetails and, on any status !== OK or null place, just `return`s with no user feedback. The click handler (line 224-232) has already called hideResults() and set the input value before fetchDetails runs, so there's no remaining UI cue. Contrast with renderPredictions which at least shows 'No matches.' for ZERO_RESULTS.
- **Repro:** 1. Exhaust the daily Places quota (or block the Places Details endpoint via devtools). 2. Type a query, get predictions, click one. 3. Observe: dropdown closes, input keeps the name, but no marker/bubble/error appears.
- **Suggested fix:** In the getDetails callback's failure branch, surface a lightweight message (showLiquidAlert(t('map.couldNotLoadPlace')) or re-open the dropdown with an inline error row), and ideally keep the dropdown open on failure so the user can retry another result.
- **Verifier:** fetchDetails (mapSearch.ts:178-179) bare-returns on status!==OK||!place with no feedback, and the click handler already ran hideResults() (230) and overwrote the input (229) before calling fetchDetails (231), leaving no UI cue — real but a rare edge for a just-returned prediction, P3.

### DSGN-061 — [P3][design-ux] Places result on the to-do list double-pins on the map — POI/search pin and to-do pin overlap because skipPlaceIds is never passed

_maps · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/HeroMap.tsx:654`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:44`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:188`
- **Symptom:** When a place is both surfaced by an active POI pill (or the search marker) AND on the to-do list, the map shows two stacked markers at the same coordinate — the colored POI circle and the purple to-do square — overlapping and fighting for clicks. The to-do module was explicitly built to avoid this.
- **Root cause:** paintTodoMarkers supports a skipPlaceIds Set (documented at todoMarkers.ts:44-46, applied at line 188-189 'so the map doesn't double-pin'), but the only caller, repaintTodoMarkers in HeroMap.tsx:654-660, never passes skipPlaceIds. The set of currently-painted POI/search place_ids (available from placesMarkers / searchMarker) is never collected and forwarded.
- **Repro:** 1. Add a restaurant to the to-do list. 2. Turn on the Restaurants pill. 3. That restaurant now renders both a colored POI circle and a purple to-do square at the same spot.
- **Suggested fix:** Build a Set of place_ids currently painted by active POI pills (and the search marker) and pass it as skipPlaceIds to paintTodoMarkers; recompute and repaint on pill toggle so the dedup stays correct as pills change.
- **Verifier:** paintTodoMarkers honours skipPlaceIds (todoMarkers.ts:46,189) but the sole caller repaintTodoMarkers (HeroMap.tsx:652-661) never passes it and never collects placesMarkers/searchMarker place_ids, so a place that is both POI/search-pinned and on the to-do list draws two overlapping markers — minor visual, P3.

### DSGN-062 — [P3][design-ux] Map search bar offers an interactive search box that silently does nothing when the Maps API key is missing/blocked

_maps · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.72_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:67`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/MapSearchBar.tsx:43`, `frontend/templates/index.html:134`
- **Symptom:** When Maps fails to initialize, the search strip still renders with the placeholder 'Search any place on the map…'. The user types and gets nothing — no dropdown, no clear button (it never toggles), no 'search unavailable' message. The control looks functional but is inert.
- **Root cause:** If GOOGLE_MAPS_API_KEY is unset, index.html:134 loads the Maps JS with an empty key, so google.maps never initializes and whenGoogleMapsReady() rejects. wireMapSearchBanner early-returns at mapSearch.ts:67 (no AutocompleteService), so NONE of the input/clear/results listeners are attached, but MapSearchBar.tsx unconditionally renders the input strip. There is no disabled/placeholder-changed/hidden state for the Maps-down case.
- **Repro:** 1. Run with GOOGLE_MAPS_API_KEY unset (or block maps.googleapis.com). 2. Open a trip on Home. 3. The map area is blank but the search bar renders; typing does nothing and no feedback is shown.
- **Suggested fix:** When google.maps/Places is unavailable, hide or disable the search bar (and POI pills), or swap the placeholder to a localized 'Map search unavailable' and mark the input disabled, so the affordance matches reality.
- **Verifier:** index.html:134 loads Maps JS with key={{ google_maps_api_key }} (empty if unset) and wireMapSearchBanner early-returns at mapSearch.ts:67 when AutocompleteService is absent (no listeners attached), yet MapSearchBar.tsx renders the input strip unconditionally with no disabled/hidden state — real but only under a rare misconfig, P3.

### DSGN-063 — [P3][perf] wireMapSearchBanner leaks a document-level click listener on every HeroMap mount (never removed in cleanup)

_maps · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:246`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/HeroMap.tsx:632`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/HeroMap.tsx:852`
- **Symptom:** Each time the Home map mounts (navigate away to another tab and back, or the cold-load async-Maps retry), a new global document 'click' listener is registered and never removed. Over a long session of navigating in/out of Home, stale listeners accumulate; each captures a prior render's resultsEl/map closures, slowly increasing memory and per-click work.
- **Root cause:** mapSearch.ts:246 attaches document.addEventListener('click', …) but wireMapSearchBanner returns void and provides no teardown. HeroMap's effect cleanup (HeroMap.tsx:852-865) only removes the poiTogglesEl listener; it has no reference to remove the mapSearch document listener. The input/results/clear listeners are on React-owned nodes that get GC'd, but the document-level one persists.
- **Repro:** 1. Open Home, then navigate to Collections, then back to Home; repeat several times. 2. In devtools, inspect getEventListeners(document) (or take heap snapshots) — the click listener count grows by one per Home mount and never drops.
- **Suggested fix:** Have wireMapSearchBanner return a disposer that removes the document click listener (and clears any pending typingTimer), and call it from HeroMap's effect cleanup; or attach the click-outside handler to a component-owned wrapper that React unmounts instead of document.
- **Verifier:** mapSearch.ts:246 attaches document.addEventListener('click',…) and returns void with no teardown; HeroMap's cleanup (852-865) only removes the poiTogglesEl listener, so each navigate('home') remount adds another permanent document-level click handler — real leak but the handler is cheap (getElementById + contains), P3.

### DSGN-064 — [P3][inconsistency] Map search + POI use deprecated legacy Places API (AutocompleteService / PlacesService) — future breakage risk

_maps · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:69`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/mapSearch.ts:175`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/HeroMap.tsx:243`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/HeroMap.tsx:467`
- **Symptom:** All map place lookups depend on Google's legacy Places JS classes that Google marked deprecated (March 2025, no longer recommended for new keys) — AutocompleteService.getPlacePredictions, PlacesService.getDetails, and PlacesService.nearbySearch. New API keys / projects may not have these enabled, and Google has signaled eventual end-of-support, which would silently break search and POI pills (both already fail to null with no user-facing message).
- **Root cause:** mapSearch.ts uses new google.maps.places.AutocompleteService() + svc.getDetails; HeroMap.tsx uses new google.maps.places.PlacesService(map) + svc.nearbySearch with RankBy.DISTANCE / radius. No migration to the newer AutocompleteSuggestion / Place (importLibrary('places')) classes exists.
- **Repro:** Provision a brand-new Google Maps key with only the newer Places API (New) enabled and no legacy Places API: the home map search returns no predictions and POI pills drop no markers, with the failure swallowed (early-return / empty array).
- **Suggested fix:** Plan a migration to the new Places library (AutocompleteSuggestion.fetchAutocompleteSuggestions, Place.fetchFields, searchNearby). In the interim, detect the deprecated-API-disabled case and surface a degraded-mode message instead of silently returning nothing.
- **Verifier:** mapSearch.ts uses new google.maps.places.AutocompleteService() (69) + getDetails (175) and HeroMap.tsx uses new google.maps.places.PlacesService(map) (243) + nearbySearch (467); grep confirms no AutocompleteSuggestion/importLibrary/Place migration exists — these are Google-deprecated legacy classes, still functional so future-risk only, P3.

### DSGN-065 — [P3][perf] Per-item uploaded files are orphaned on disk on photo/doc removal, cover swap, and document 'Replace'

_media · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.78_

- **Files:** `src/routes/trips.py:698`, `src/helpers.py:56`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/tripMediaModals.ts:484`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/trip.ts:463`
- **Symptom:** Every removed-or-replaced upload leaves its file under /static/uploads/<user>/ forever. Heavy users (and the 'replace cover 5 times' flow) accumulate dead files indefinitely — unbounded disk growth on PythonAnywhere's quota'd filesystem.
- **Root cause:** Disk cleanup (`collect_trip_upload_paths` + `delete_upload_files`) is wired ONLY into whole-trip and whole-day delete. `update_trip_media` (trips.py:698) just overwrites the photos_json/documents_json column and never diffs the old array to rm the now-unreferenced file; the cover-swap path (trip.ts:463) overwrites `trip.coverUrl` with no cleanup of the prior cover. The 'Replace' document flow (tripMediaModals.ts:856) uploads a new file and overwrites the url, orphaning the old one.
- **Repro:** Add a trip photo (file lands on disk) → remove it from the Photos modal → the file remains under /static/uploads/<user>/. Repeat to grow the dir without bound.
- **Suggested fix:** On the media POST, diff the previous JSON array against the new one server-side and rm files that (a) drop out of the array and (b) are not referenced by any other trip/day/expense of the owner. Same for cover swap. Alternatively run a periodic GC that walks the owner's upload dir and deletes files not referenced by any owned row.
- **Verifier:** collect_trip_upload_paths/delete_upload_files (helpers.py:56) are wired only into whole-trip/whole-day delete; update_trip_media (trips.py:698-824) overwrites photos_json/documents_json with no old-array diff or file rm, cover swap overwrites trip.coverUrl with no cleanup (trip.ts:463), and document Replace overwrites url after upload (tripMediaModals.ts:856-858) — all leak files on disk; storage/lingering-access only, P3 confirmed.

### DSGN-066 — [P3][design-ux] Keyboard-avoidance only lifts modal bottom-sheets, not focused inline inputs in long non-modal forms

_mobile · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/keyboard-avoidance.ts:53`, `frontend/static/js/src/keyboard-avoidance.ts:55`
- **Symptom:** On iOS, focusing an input near the bottom of a long NON-modal page (e.g. an inline form below the fold) can leave it under the on-screen keyboard; --kb-offset is only consumed by .modal-overlay.
- **Root cause:** \_update() writes --kb-offset globally but only the .modal-overlay rule uses it (padding-bottom); non-modal inputs rely on the browser's native scroll-into-view, which iOS does imperfectly for custom-scrolled documents.
- **Repro:** iOS Safari: open a long page with a text input near the bottom (non-modal), tap it — the field can sit behind the keyboard.
- **Suggested fix:** On focusin of an input/textarea, scrollIntoView({block:'center'}) when --kb-offset>0; or apply the offset to the scroll container, not just modals.

### DSGN-067 — [P3][design-ux] Pull-to-refresh trigger threshold (~140px of finger travel) is heavier than native

_mobile · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.55_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pullToRefresh.ts:47`, `frontend/static/js/src/pullToRefresh.ts:52`
- **Symptom:** The pull needed to trigger a refresh feels notably longer than the native iOS/Android gesture, so some users won't discover it.
- **Root cause:** TRIGGER_THRESHOLD_PX is 70 measured AFTER PULL_RESISTANCE=0.5 is applied, i.e. ~140px of actual finger travel; native is ~70-80px.
- **Repro:** On mobile, pull down at the top of Home — it takes a long drag to arm the spinner.
- **Suggested fix:** Lower the effective threshold (e.g. threshold 50 or resistance 0.6) and/or add a haptic/visual 'release to refresh' state at the arm point (the is-armed class exists; surface it more).

### DSGN-069 — [P3][inconsistency] Following someone via the Friends page emits a 'Friend Request' notification whose body says 'started following you'

_notifications · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.82_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/friends/Friends.tsx:225-247`, `src/routes/friends.py:186-209`, `src/routes/friends.py:175-182`
- **Symptom:** When user A follows user B from the Friends page search, B receives a notification with title 'Friend Request' (hardcoded English) but body '{A} started following you.' — a contradictory, English-only title for what is actually a one-way follow under Model B. Non-English users get a localized body under an English 'Friend Request' heading.
- **Root cause:** Friends.tsx:232 still posts to the legacy /api/friends/add, whose handler calls \_follow(..., source='friend_request') (friends.py:207). \_follow inserts a notification with type='friend_request' and title 'Friend Request' when source != 'followed_you' (friends.py:179-181), while the message is always 'started following you.'. The live /api/follows/<id> path (used by the profile FollowButton) correctly uses type='followed_you' + title 'New follower'; the Friends page uses the legacy façade, producing the mismatched 'Friend Request' label. The title is the server's literal string, so the frontend's t()-based title fallback never localizes it.
- **Repro:** 1. As A, open Friends, search for B, click the follow/add button (fires /api/friends/add). 2. As B (ideally with UI language = ES/FR/PT), open the bell. 3. See a notification titled 'Friend Request' (English) with body 'A started following you' (localized) — title contradicts body and is not translated.
- **Suggested fix:** Point Friends.tsx follow action at /api/follows/<id> (the Model-B path), or change friends.py \_follow to always use type='followed_you' + title 'New follower' regardless of legacy `source`. Either way the recipient sees a single consistent, localizable 'New follower' notification.
- **Verifier:** Friends.tsx:232 posts to /api/friends/add whose handler calls \_follow(..., source='friend_request') (friends.py:207), and \_follow sets title to 'New follower' only when source=='followed_you' else 'Friend Request' (friends.py:180) while the message is always 'started following you.' (friends.py:181) — vs the /api/follows/<id> path which uses type='followed_you'+'New follower' (follows.py:134); a cosmetic title/body mismatch via the legacy facade, no functional harm, hence P3.

### DSGN-070 — [P3][design-ux] settled_up / settled_up_reverted notification clicks dump the user on Home instead of the trip's Settlements

_notifications · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/bootstrap/notifications.ts:259-355`, `src/routes/settlements.py:434-438`
- **Symptom:** Clicking 'X settled €50 with you for Trip Y' (or 'X reverted a settlement ...') navigates to Home, not to the Settlements view for that trip — the user is told to 'confirm with them' but lands nowhere useful.
- **Root cause:** handleNotificationClick's switch has no case for 'settled_up' or 'settled_up_reverted', so both fall to `default: navigate(PAGES.HOME)` (notifications.ts:352-354). The function's own docstring (notifications.ts:261-263) states related_id is a trip_id for settled_up/settled_up_reverted, so the data needed to route to the trip's settlement page is present but unused.
- **Repro:** 1. Have a companion settle up with you on Trip Y (or revert one). 2. Open the bell, click the settlement notification. 3. You land on Home rather than the Settlements page for Trip Y.
- **Suggested fix:** Add cases for 'settled_up' and 'settled_up_reverted' that set the active trip to related_id and navigate to the Settlements page (mirroring how trip-scoped notifications resolve), so the user can immediately confirm/dispute the transfer.
- **Verifier:** handleNotificationClick's switch (notifications.ts:294-355) has no case for settled_up/settled_up_reverted so both hit `default: navigate(PAGES.HOME)` (line 353), even though the docstring (lines 261-262) states related_id is the trip_id and a PAGES.SETTLEMENT route exists (constants.ts:21, router.ts:178) — the data to route correctly is present but unused; minor misdirection (still lands somewhere valid), so P3.

### DSGN-071 — [P3][perf] Unread notifications are never cleaned up — unbounded growth behind the LIMIT 50 window

_notifications · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.70_

- **Files:** `src/main.py:781-790`, `src/routes/notifications.py:51-56`
- **Symptom:** A user who never clicks or 'Mark all read's their notifications accumulates unread rows forever. The list endpoint only ever returns the newest 50 (notifications.py:55), so older unread rows become invisible yet keep inflating the totalUnread badge (which always shows '9+' once over 9) and the table grows without bound for inactive-but-pinged users.
- **Root cause:** The maintenance sweep deletes only `is_read = 1 AND created_at < -30 days` (main.py:786-789). Unread rows are intentionally preserved ('so the user's bell keeps surfacing them'), but with no age ceiling and a 50-row read cap, ancient unread notifications neither surface nor get reclaimed.
- **Repro:** 1. Be a popular user (many followers/engagements) and never open the bell. 2. Over weeks, accumulate hundreds of unread rows. 3. The bell always shows the newest 50; the badge sticks at '9+'; the table row count for that user grows unbounded and old unread rows are dead weight.
- **Suggested fix:** Add a generous age ceiling for unread rows too (e.g. delete is_read=0 older than 180 days), or cap stored notifications per user (keep newest N) on insert, so the table can't grow unbounded while still giving users a long grace window to act.
- **Verifier:** The maintenance sweep deletes only `is_read = 1 AND created_at < -30 days` (main.py:786-789) with unread rows intentionally preserved (comment lines 781-782), while the read query caps at LIMIT 50 (notifications.py:55) — so unread rows beyond the most-recent 50 neither surface nor get reclaimed; a genuine slow-burn growth issue but the COUNT/LIMIT keep reads cheap, so P3.

### DSGN-072 — [P3][design-ux] Trip-wide photos tagged to a day are embedded twice (in the day card AND the photo gallery)

_pdf · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:893`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:1076`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:1088`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:887`
- **Symptom:** When photo embedding is on, any photo the user attached to a specific day appears TWICE in the PDF — once inline under that day's plan, and again in the standalone Photos gallery at the end. The section comment promises 'any per-day photos NOT already inlined in the day cards', but the dedup never happens, so the document is padded with duplicates and is larger than it should be.
- **Root cause:** The route merges trip-level photos that carry a `dayId` into each day's `photos` list so the day cards render them (**init**.py:1076-1088). But the standalone gallery builds from `trip_photos` = the FULL photos_json list (**init**.py:251 → used at :893 `_collect_photos(trip_photos, ...)`), with no exclusion of the dayId-tagged entries that were just inlined. So a photo with a dayId is collected for both the day card and the gallery.
- **Repro:** 1. Create a trip with a day. 2. Add a photo to that specific day (lands in photos_json with a dayId). 3. Export the PDF with both day plan and Photos on. 4. The same photo appears under the day AND in the closing Photos gallery.
- **Suggested fix:** Build the gallery from only the trip photos WITHOUT a dayId (or subtract the set of dayId-tagged srcs that were merged into days), matching the section's stated 'not already inlined' contract. e.g. `gallery_entries = [p for p in trip_photos if not (isinstance(p, dict) and p.get('dayId'))]`.

### DSGN-073 — [P3][i18n] Per-day map labels and budget scope labels render in English regardless of locale

_pdf · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.90_

- **Files:** `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:505`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:1126`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:1128`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:1130`, `src/routes/pdf/_i18n.py:62`, `src/routes/pdf/_i18n.py:63`
- **Symptom:** A French/Spanish/Portuguese user exporting a PDF gets two English strings leaking into an otherwise-translated document: (1) the overview-map kicker 'EVERY DAY ON ONE MAP · N PINS', and (2) every auto-derived budget label uses English 'Overall' / 'Category budget' (e.g. a budget row reads 'Overall · Bruno' instead of 'Global · Bruno' in FR).
- **Root cause:** The whole PDF was localised via the `_STRINGS` table (PDF-5), but these two paths hardcode English literals. **init**.py:505 builds the kicker with a raw f-string + 'PIN'/'PINS'. **init**.py:1119-1130 derives the budget label using literal 'Overall' (:1128), 'Category budget' (:1126,:1130) — even though the i18n table already defines `budget_overall` and `budget_category` keys in all four locales (\_i18n.py:62-63 and equivalents), which were clearly added to be used here but never wired up.
- **Repro:** 1. Switch UI language to French. 2. Create a trip with day pins + a category-scoped budget (no explicit label). 3. Export PDF with Days(+pins) and Budgets on. 4. The overview map header reads 'EVERY DAY ON ONE MAP' and the budget row label reads 'Category budget'/'Overall' in English.
- **Suggested fix:** Route the overview kicker through `tr` (add e.g. `every_day_on_one_map` / a pins-count string to \_STRINGS). Replace the budget scope literals with `tr('budget_overall')` / `tr('budget_category')` (the keys already exist in all locales).

### DSGN-074 — [P3][design-ux] 'Per-day maps' checkbox is silently ignored when 'Day-by-day plan' is unchecked

_pdf · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.82_

- **Files:** `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:448`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:469`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:523`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/pdf.ts:66`
- **Symptom:** The export modal exposes 'Per-day maps' as an independent checkbox, but if the user unchecks 'Day-by-day plan' while leaving 'Per-day maps' checked, NO maps appear in the PDF — neither the all-days overview map nor the per-day mini-maps. The checkbox has no effect, with no explanation.
- **Root cause:** In the builder, both the overview pins map (**init**.py:469) and the per-day mini-map (**init**.py:523) are nested INSIDE `if opt('includeDays') and days_renderable:` (**init**.py:448). So `includeDayPins` is only honoured when `includeDays` is also true. The modal (modals/pdf.ts:66-69) presents the two as independent toggles, creating a state the backend silently drops.
- **Repro:** 1. Open the PDF export modal. 2. Uncheck 'Day-by-day plan', keep 'Per-day maps' checked. 3. Download. 4. The PDF has no maps section at all despite the per-day-maps box being ticked.
- **Suggested fix:** Either disable/auto-uncheck 'Per-day maps' in the modal when 'Day-by-day plan' is off (and add a hint), or in the builder allow the overview map to render under `includeDayPins` independently of `includeDays`. Disabling the dependent checkbox in the UI is the lower-risk fix.

### DSGN-075 — [P3][i18n] AI-plan PDF section is unreachable dead code carrying untranslated English (latent)

_pdf · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.70_

- **Files:** `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:548`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:555`, `src/routes/pdf/__init__.py:583`, `frontend/static/js/src/modals/pdf.ts:136`
- **Symptom:** The PDF builder has a full 'AI suggestions' section (~67 lines, **init**.py:548-615) gated on `options['aiPlan']`, but the production export modal never forwards an `aiPlan` array — it only sends the checkbox booleans + locale (modals/pdf.ts:136-142). So this section can never render for real users. If it ever IS wired up, it ships hardcoded English: the kicker 'Gemini-generated plan kept alongside…' (:555-556) and slot labels 'BREAKFAST'/'LUNCH'/'DINNER'/'SIGHTS' (:583-598) bypass the i18n table.
- **Root cause:** The frontend modal collects only `input[type=checkbox]` values + `options.locale` (modals/pdf.ts:133-142); no code path populates `options.aiPlan`. The builder's `ai_plan_extra` branch therefore always gets an empty list in production. The dead branch also predates/ignores the PDF-5 i18n work for its inline strings.
- **Repro:** Not user-reproducible (the trigger is never sent). Verify by grepping the frontend for `aiPlan` — it appears in AI page state and types but never in the PDF modal POST body.
- **Suggested fix:** Either remove the dead AI-plan branch from the builder, or, if it's intended to ship, wire the modal to forward the cached `activeTrip.aiPlan` and route its inline strings ('BREAKFAST'/'LUNCH'/'DINNER'/'SIGHTS' + the kicker) through the `tr` translator before exposing it.

### DSGN-076 — [P3][inconsistency] DELETE /api/expenses/<id> is the only mutating route with no per-route rate limit (relies solely on the 200/min global default)

_security · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `src/routes/expenses.py:311-314`, `src/extensions.py:23-27`
- **Symptom:** Every sibling write/delete route carries an explicit tight @limiter.limit (e.g. delete_day 60/min, delete_budget 30/min, delete_settlement 30/min, upsert_expense 120/min). delete_expense has only @require_auth + @retry_on_lock, so it falls back to the broad 200/min default — looser than every comparable endpoint. A leaked token could fire soft-delete tombstone writes at 200/min, tarpitting the single SQLite writer lock harder than the analogous 30-60/min siblings allow.
- **Root cause:** Missing @limiter.limit decorator on delete_expense; the global default_limits=['200 per minute'] (extensions.py:25) silently covers it but at a much higher rate than intended for a write path.
- **Repro:** Inspect routes/expenses.py:311-314 — no @limiter.limit between the route and the function, unlike delete_day at days.py:193-196.
- **Suggested fix:** Add @limiter.limit("60 per minute") (or 30/min to match delete_budget/delete_settlement) to delete_expense for consistency with the other delete routes.

### DSGN-077 — [P3][inconsistency] upsert_expense uses `request.json or {}` instead of the SEC-2 json_body() helper, so a POST without application/json content-type 415s/400s before the isinstance guard

_security · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.60_

- **Files:** `src/routes/expenses.py:37-42`, `src/helpers.py:16-28`
- **Symptom:** Every other write route migrated to the SEC-2 `json_body()` helper (which returns {} for non-JSON / non-dict / wrong-content-type bodies). upsert_expense still uses `data = request.json or {}` with a manual isinstance check. In Flask 2.1+ the `request.json` property raises (415 Unsupported Media Type / 400) when Content-Type isn't JSON, so a malformed client hits a framework error path instead of the route's own clean 400, diverging from the documented SEC-2 contract that the whole write surface was supposed to share.
- **Root cause:** The SEC-2 sweep (json_body across write routes) missed expenses.py — it kept the legacy `request.json or {}` idiom that the helper was introduced to replace.
- **Repro:** curl -X POST /api/expenses with a body but no Content-Type header (and a valid Bearer token) — behavior differs from /api/days, /api/budgets, /api/trips which all funnel through json_body().
- **Suggested fix:** Replace `data = request.json or {}` + the isinstance branch with `data = json_body()` (import already pattern-matched elsewhere), matching the rest of the write routes.

### DSGN-078 — [P3][design-ux] Factory Reset wipes data but silently re-logs the user in (HttpOnly session cookie survives)

_settings · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Settings.tsx:186`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Settings.tsx:210`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Settings.tsx:214`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/core.ts:57`
- **Symptom:** After 'Factory Reset / Erase Everything', the app reloads and the user is silently signed back into the same (now-empty) account rather than landing on the login wall. The code even sets STATE.user = null first, implying a sign-out was intended.
- **Root cause:** confirmResetApp (Settings.tsx:186) DELETEs /api/user-data, clears local STATE (including STATE.user = null, line 210), then does localStorage.clear() + location.reload() (lines 214-215). The session JWT lives in an HttpOnly `gg_session` cookie that JS cannot clear and that only /api/auth/logout invalidates (api/core.ts:57). location.reload() therefore re-runs restoreSession(), which succeeds on the surviving cookie, so the user is re-authenticated. The server data is genuinely wiped (so this is not data corruption), but the behavior contradicts the 'Erase Everything' framing and the explicit STATE.user=null.
- **Repro:** 1) Log in. 2) Settings → Data Management → Factory Reset → ERASE EVERYTHING. 3) Page reloads; instead of the login wall, you're back in the app, logged in, with empty data.
- **Suggested fix:** Before location.reload(), await a call to /api/auth/logout (the helper that clears the gg_session cookie + rotates token_jti) so the reload genuinely returns the user to the login wall — matching the destructive copy and the STATE.user=null intent.

### DSGN-079 — [P3][i18n] Edit-Category modal mixes localized and hardcoded-English strings

_settings · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.95_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings.ts:106`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings.ts:110`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings.ts:115`
- **Symptom:** Opening 'Edit category' as a non-English user shows an English modal title 'Edit Category', an English 'Cancel' button, and an English 'Category name' input placeholder — while the Save button right next to Cancel IS translated, making the mismatch obvious.
- **Root cause:** openEditCategoryModal (settings.ts:95) builds the modal via showModal innerHTML with hardcoded literals: the <h2> 'Edit Category' (line 106), the input placeholder='Category name' (line 110), and the Cancel button text (line 115). Only the submit button uses t('settings.editCategorySaveBtn') (line 114). This legacy helper was left in settings.ts during the React migration and never fully i18n'd.
- **Repro:** 1) Set language to es/fr/pt. 2) Settings → Personalization → Categories. 3) Click the edit (pencil) icon on any category. 4) Observe 'Edit Category' title, 'Cancel' button, and 'Category name' placeholder remain English while 'Save' is translated.
- **Suggested fix:** Add/route through existing settings.\* keys for the modal title, the name placeholder (a categoryNamePlaceholder key already exists), and Cancel (common.cancel exists), replacing the three literals with t(...).

### DSGN-080 — [P3][inconsistency] Theme and POI customization are device-local while Language syncs across devices, despite identical Settings presentation

_settings · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.70_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:59`, `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:109`, `frontend/static/js/src/i18n.ts:192`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settings/Settings.tsx:496`
- **Symptom:** A user customizes their theme and POI pill filters/visibility/anchoring on desktop, then opens the app on their phone — those preferences are all back to defaults. But the Language they picked on desktop DOES follow them to the phone. Two settings that sit in the same 'General settings' area with the same pill UI behave differently with no indication.
- **Root cause:** STATE.preferences (theme, mapDefaultPois, poiFilters, poiVisible, poiAnchoring, pillEpicenters, enabledPois) is persisted ONLY to localStorage (state.ts:59 'Stored on this device only'; subscribe(STATE_CHANGED, saveState) at state.ts:438). The server has no preferences column. Language is special-cased: setLocale (i18n.ts:192) additionally POSTs /api/profile/update {language}, stored in users.language and hydrated into STATE.preferences.locale on boot (main.ts:123-129). So locale is the only cross-device preference; theme/POI silently are not. The theme/POI copy doesn't promise sync, so this is an inconsistency rather than a broken promise, but the parallel UI invites the wrong expectation.
- **Repro:** 1) On device A: Settings → General → Appearance pick Dark; → Map pills hide a pill + raise a rating filter; → Language pick Français. 2) Log in on device B. 3) Observe language is Français (synced) but theme is back to System and all POI customizations are gone.
- **Suggested fix:** Either persist the rest of STATE.preferences server-side alongside language (a small preferences JSON blob on the user row, hydrated on boot) so all of General settings follows the user, or add a short 'applies to this device only' note under the Theme + Map-pills sections to set expectations and remove the implied parity with Language.

### DSGN-081 — [P3][inconsistency] Admin dashboard: per-user trip count includes archived trips while global total excludes them

_settings · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `src/routes/admin.py:136`, `src/routes/admin.py:202`
- **Symptom:** In the Developer dashboard, summing the per-user 'Trips' column does not match the top 'Total Trips' stat, because the two count trips with different rules. An operator reconciling the numbers sees an unexplained discrepancy.
- **Root cause:** The global totalTrips (admin.py:136-141) counts only NON-archived trips (JOIN trip_members on the owner row WHERE COALESCE(is_archived,0)=0). The per-user roster's trip_count (admin.py:202) is `(SELECT COUNT(*) FROM trips t WHERE t.user_id = u.id)` — every owned trip regardless of archive state. The two definitions diverge for any user with archived trips.
- **Repro:** 1) As admin, archive one of your trips. 2) Settings → Developer. 3) Compare 'Total Trips' (decremented by the archive) against your row's 'Trips' count (unchanged) — they no longer reconcile across the roster.
- **Suggested fix:** Make the per-user trip_count subquery use the same active-trip definition as the global counter (JOIN trip_members on the owner row WHERE COALESCE(is_archived,0)=0), or add separate active/archived columns, so the dashboard is internally consistent.

### DSGN-082 — [P3][i18n] Settlement History groups rows by UTC calendar date — evening settlements show under the wrong day for non-UTC users, and same-day rows have unstable ordering

_settlements · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settlement/viewData.ts:178`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settlement/SettlementView.tsx:364`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settlement/SettlementView.tsx:382`, `migrations/versions/0c7a67724fda_baseline.py:45`
- **Symptom:** A settlement a user records in the evening (or any time whose UTC calendar date differs from their local date) is filed under the wrong day header — e.g. recorded ~22:00 local on Jun 4 in a UTC-3 zone is stamped 2026-06-05 in UTC, so it shows under 'Tomorrow's' date / not under 'Today'. Conversely a late-night settle in a UTC+ zone can land under 'Yesterday'. Additionally, multiple settlements on the same day are sorted only by the (date-only) key, so their relative order within the day is arbitrary rather than newest-first.
- **Root cause:** collectSettlementHistory (viewData.ts:178) derives the grouping/sort key as `date: (s.createdAt || '').slice(0,10)`. createdAt comes from settlements.created_at, which is SQLite `DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP` = UTC (baseline.py:45). Slicing the first 10 chars yields the UTC calendar date, not the viewer's local date. The History tab then compares that key against `new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)` (also UTC) for Today/Yesterday labels (SettlementView.tsx:370-373) and sorts by `new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date)` (viewData.ts:184), which—because the time component was dropped—cannot order same-day rows.
- **Repro:** In a browser set to a UTC-offset timezone (e.g. America/Sao_Paulo, UTC-3), record a settlement at ~22:30 local. Open History — the row appears under tomorrow's date header instead of 'Today'. Record two settlements minutes apart the same day — their order in the list is not guaranteed newest-first.
- **Suggested fix:** Group/sort settlement history on the FULL local timestamp: keep `s.createdAt` (the full ISO) for sorting (sort by Date(createdAt) descending), and compute the day-bucket key from the local date (e.g. new Date(createdAt) → local YYYY-MM-DD) rather than slicing the UTC string. Apply the same local-date derivation to the Today/Yesterday comparison.
- **Verifier:** collectSettlementHistory sets date:(s.createdAt||'').slice(0,10) (viewData.ts:178) off created_at which is DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP=UTC (baseline.py:45), and the History tab labels Today/Yesterday by comparing to new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10) (also UTC, SettlementView.tsx:370) and sorts on the time-stripped date (viewData.ts:184) so same-day rows can't be ordered — real but purely cosmetic display drift.

### DSGN-083 — [P3][i18n] Hardcoded English 'Couldn't undo' toast on settlement-delete failure (i18n gap)

_settlements · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.92_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/settlement/actions.ts:261`, `frontend/static/js/src/locales/en.ts:651`
- **Symptom:** A non-English user (es/fr/pt) who hits a failed settlement undo sees an English-only toast 'Couldn't undo: <error>' / 'Couldn't undo: Network error', while the rest of the settlement UI (including the very similar create-failure toast) is localized.
- **Root cause:** deleteSettlement's failure branch builds the message as a raw template literal: `Couldn't undo: ${result.error || 'Network error'}` (actions.ts:261) instead of going through t(). The codebase already has the localized sibling `settlement.toastSettlementFailed: 'Settlement failed: {error}'` (en.ts:651, mirrored across locales) used on the create path — the delete path simply wasn't wired to an equivalent key. Because it's a hardcoded literal it bypasses the compile-time Translations check entirely.
- **Repro:** Switch the app language to Spanish/French/Portuguese. As a non-owner recipient of a settlement (who is forbidden from deleting), attempt Undo on that row → server returns 403 → toast shows the English string 'Couldn't undo: Forbidden' regardless of locale.
- **Suggested fix:** Add a localized key (e.g. settlement.toastUnsettleFailed: "Couldn't undo: {error}" plus a toastUnsettleFailedNetwork fallback) to all four locale files and replace the literal at actions.ts:261 with t('settlement.toastUnsettleFailed', { error: result.error || t('settlement.toastUnsettleFailedNetwork') }).
- **Verifier:** deleteSettlement's failure branch shows a raw literal `Couldn't undo: ${result.error || 'Network error'}` (actions.ts:261) bypassing t(), whereas the localized sibling settlement.toastSettlementFailed exists (en.ts:651) and is used on the create path (actions.ts:177) — a genuine but minor untranslated-string gap on an error toast.

### DSGN-084 — [P3][design-ux] Revoked / expired / archived share page still renders the "I want this trip" clone CTA that then fails with a generic error

_sharing · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.83_

- **Files:** `frontend/templates/share.html:379`, `frontend/templates/share.html:391`, `src/main.py:1085`, `src/routes/trips.py:1550`, `frontend/static/js/src/bootstrap/clone-intent.ts:48`
- **Symptom:** When a share link is revoked, points at a deleted trip, or the owner has archived the trip, the page renders the friendly 'This trip isn't available' state — but still shows the 'Like this trip? ✨ I want this trip' button. Clicking it makes the user sign in (if needed) and then fails with a generic 'could not clone' toast, a confusing dead-end.
- **Root cause:** The .share-cta block including the clone link (share.html:379-393) is OUTSIDE the {% if days %}/{% if cost %} guards, and the 404 render path in main.py:1085-1101 still passes canonical_url, so the CTA href '/?cloneFromShare=<token>' is emitted on the unavailable page too. clone_trip_from_share_token returns 404 (revoked/deleted) or 410 (archived) (trips.py:1548-1553), and attemptPendingClone surfaces only the generic t('errors.cloneFailedFromCollections') (clone-intent.ts:48-51) with no distinct 'this trip is no longer available' message.
- **Repro:** 1) Share a trip, copy the link, then Unshare it (or archive the trip). 2) Open the link → 'This trip isn't available'. 3) The 'I want this trip' button is still shown. 4) Click it, sign in → generic clone-failed toast; the user can't tell the trip was revoked.
- **Suggested fix:** Only render the .share-cta clone button when a real payload exists (wrap it in {% if days or trip.coverUrl %} or pass an explicit `available` flag from the route and gate on it). On the unavailable page show only 'Open the app'. Optionally map the 410/404 from the clone endpoint to a dedicated 'This trip is no longer available' string in attemptPendingClone.
- **Verifier:** The .share-cta block with the clone link (share.html:379-393) is OUTSIDE the {% if days %}/{% if cost %} guards (which close at 377/329) and the 404 render path passes canonical_url (main.py:1100), so /?cloneFromShare=<token> is emitted on the unavailable page; the clone endpoints return 404/410 (trips.py:1548-1553) and attemptPendingClone surfaces only the generic t('errors.cloneFailedFromCollections') on !res.ok (clone-intent.ts:48-51, 68) with no distinct unavailable message.

### DSGN-085 — [P3][i18n] Public share page is hardcoded English despite full en/es/fr/pt app support

_sharing · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.78_

- **Files:** `frontend/templates/share.html:2`, `frontend/templates/share.html:289`, `frontend/templates/share.html:332`, `frontend/templates/share.html:391`, `src/main.py:1072`
- **Symptom:** Every recipient of a share link sees an English-only page — 'Shared by', 'The path', 'Trip Hub', 'Day N', 'Morning/Afternoon/Evening', '💡 Tip', '… view/views', 'Like this trip?', '✨ I want this trip', 'Open the app', and the 'This trip isn't available' empty state — even though the product ships full Spanish/French/Portuguese locales and the recipient is frequently in a non-English locale (links are pasted into WhatsApp/iMessage across languages).
- **Root cause:** share_page (main.py:1072) renders share.html with no locale resolution; <html lang="en"> is hardcoded (share.html:2) and all visible copy is literal English in the template. There is no Accept-Language handling and no server-side string table (unlike the PDF route, which got server-side i18n in PDF-5). The /t/<code> template-preview page shares the same English-only posture, so this is at least consistent, but it remains a real gap for a public, shareable surface.
- **Repro:** 1) Set device/browser language to Spanish. 2) Open any /share/<token> link. 3) Page renders entirely in English (section labels, day labels, CTAs, empty state).

Set <html lang> dynamically. Apply to template.html too for parity.
- **Verifier:** share_page (main.py:1072) does no locale resolution and passes no string table; <html lang="en"> is hardcoded (share.html:2) and every visible string is literal English in the template ('Shared by', 'The path', 'Morning/Afternoon/Evening', 'Like this trip?', 'I want this trip', 'Open the app') — a real gap for a public surface, matching the audit's framing.

### DSGN-086 — [P3][perf] Per-trip POI preference keys (enabledPois / pillEpicenters / poiAnchoring) are never pruned when a trip is deleted

_state · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.80_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/bootstrap/trip-controls.ts:175`, `frontend/static/js/src/bootstrap/trip-controls.ts:192`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/collections/handlers.ts:94`, `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:109`
- **Symptom:** Every trip the user deletes (or archives-then-deletes) leaves orphaned per-trip preference entries in STATE.preferences.enabledPois[tripId], pillEpicenters[tripId], and poiAnchoring (per-pill) that are persisted to localStorage forever. Over a heavy user's lifetime these accumulate; combined with the full-STATE JSON.stringify on every save (state.ts:363) and the re-merged media arrays, this contributes to the same localStorage bloat / main-thread stringify cost the debounce was added to mitigate.
- **Root cause:** The permanent-delete handler (trip-controls.ts:174-204) prunes expenses, tripDays, settlements, budgets, and STATE.fxOverridesByTrip[trip.id] (line 192) but NOT STATE.preferences.enabledPois[trip.id] / pillEpicenters[trip.id]. The archived-trip permanent-delete path (collections/handlers.ts:94) prunes none of the per-trip preference maps at all. There is no boot-time reconciliation that drops preference keys whose tripId no longer exists in STATE.trips/archivedTrips (loadState only backfills/heals these maps, never garbage-collects stale keys — state.ts:189-207).
- **Repro:** Create trip A, toggle some POI pills on (writes enabledPois[A]) and set a search center (writes pillEpicenters[A]). Delete trip A. Inspect localStorage 'theGreatEscapeState' → preferences.enabledPois and pillEpicenters still contain A's id. Repeat across many trips to watch the maps grow unbounded.
- **Suggested fix:** In both delete paths, also `delete STATE.preferences.enabledPois[id]` and `delete STATE.preferences.pillEpicenters[id]`. Better: add a one-pass reconciliation in loadState() (after trips/archivedTrips are known) that drops any enabledPois/pillEpicenters/fxOverridesByTrip key whose tripId isn't in the current live+archived trip set — self-heals existing orphans and covers cross-device deletes.
- **Verifier:** Live-trip permanent-delete (trip-controls.ts:174-207) prunes expenses/tripDays/settlements/budgets/fxOverridesByTrip[id] but not preferences.enabledPois/pillEpicenters/poiAnchoring, and the archived-trip permanent-delete (deleteArchivedTrip, handlers.ts:116-143 — the cited line 94 was actually the restore path, but the substance holds) prunes only archivedTrips; enabledPois IS written per-trip-id (HeroMap.tsx:564) and loadState (state.ts:189-207) only type-resets these maps, never GCs stale tripId keys — a real but cosmetic localStorage leak with no functional impact since ids are unique.

### DSGN-087 — [P3][inconsistency] Legacy 🏖️ Sights icon is not healed for server-fetched media → a duplicate 'Sights' section + duplicate filter entry

_todo · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.70_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/state.ts:246`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/media.ts:204`, `frontend/static/js/src/api/media.ts:233`, `frontend/static/js/src/todoCategories.ts:81`, `frontend/static/js/src/todoCategories.ts:20`
- **Symptom:** A to-do list whose places were stored with the old 🏖️ Sights icon renders TWO 'Sights' sections (one under 🏛️, one under 🏖️) and the category filter dropdown lists 'Sights' twice. The icon-heal comment claims this is fixed on load, but it isn't for the freshly-fetched media.
- **Root cause:** The 🏖️→🏛️ heal only runs inside loadState() over localStorage data (state.ts:246). The authoritative markedPlaces for the active trip arrive LATER via fetchTripMedia(), which splices the server arrays straight into trip.markedPlaces (media.ts:204, 233) without re-running the heal. groupingIcon() normalises 📋→📍 but NOT 🏖️→🏛️ (todoCategories.ts:20), and 🏖️ is absent from CATEGORY_ORDER (todoCategories.ts:81), so a 🏖️ place forms its own trailing bucket. iconToLabel maps both 🏖️ and 🏛️ to 'Sights', producing two identically-labelled sections/filter rows.
- **Repro:** Seed a trip's marked_places_json server-side with a place carrying icon '🏖️' (or restore a pre-heal trip), open it fresh so media is fetched (not from localStorage), open /todo: two 'Sights' headers appear and the type filter shows 'Sights' twice.
- **Suggested fix:** Normalise 🏖️→🏛️ inside groupingIcon() (so grouping/filtering always collapses it), and/or re-run the marked-place heal on the arrays fetchTripMedia splices into STATE.

### DSGN-088 — [P3][i18n] Day-Detail shortlist AM/PM/Eve buttons swap and de-localise their glyphs after the first interaction

_todo · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.85_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:747`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:304`, `frontend/static/js/src/locales/en.ts:1846`
- **Symptom:** When the Day Detail modal opens, the shortlist add buttons read '☀️ AM / 🌅 PM / 🌙 Eve' (localised). The moment the user types in a plan textarea or toggles any shortlist button, the AM/PM glyphs flip (AM becomes 🌅, PM becomes ☀️) and the labels revert to hardcoded English regardless of locale, and now disagree with the day-plan tab strip (which uses ☀️ for morning, 🌅 for afternoon).
- **Root cause:** Initial render uses the i18n strings shortlistBtnAm='☀️ AM', shortlistBtnPm='🌅 PM' (en.ts:1846) — sun=morning, matching \_slotIcon at dayDetailModal.ts:304. But refreshShortlistButtons() rebuilds the label as a hardcoded literal `time==='morning' ? '🌅 AM' : time==='afternoon' ? '☀️ PM' : '🌙 Eve'` (dayDetailModal.ts:747) — sunset=morning (swapped) and not run through t(). refreshShortlistButtons runs on every input/toggle and on initial paint, overwriting the localised text.
- **Repro:** Open a numbered day's Detail modal in any locale; note the AM button shows ☀️. Type one character in a textarea (or click an AM/PM button). The AM button now shows 🌅 and PM shows ☀️ (swapped), in English, mismatching the tab-strip icons above.
- **Suggested fix:** In refreshShortlistButtons build the label from the same source as the initial render: `_slotIcon[time]` + the localised t('dayDetail.shortlistBtnAm'|'Pm'|'Eve') (strip/re-add the ✓ prefix), instead of the hardcoded swapped literals.

### DSGN-089 — [P3][i18n] Hardcoded English strings across the to-do / marked-place surfaces (not localised)

_todo · verdict: **unverified** · confidence 0.90_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/todo/Todo.tsx:643`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/todo/Todo.tsx:179`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/todo/Todo.tsx:241`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/todo/Todo.tsx:324`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:145`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/todoMarkers.ts:157`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/ai/TodoListPanel.tsx:373`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/dayDetailModal.ts:611`
- **Symptom:** Several user-visible strings on the To-do page, the home to-do map InfoWindow, the AI marked-card grid, and the Day Detail modal stay English in es/fr/pt locales: the 'Plan with AI ✦' button, the in-row and detail 'View on Google Maps →' link, the 'Open {name} on Google Maps' title/aria-label, the expand 'Hide details'/'Show details' aria-label, the to-do map InfoWindow's 'On your to-do list' pill and 'Day N · {name}' chip, and the day-checklist 'X of Y left' summary that gets re-written on toggle.
- **Root cause:** These literals are written directly in JSX/HTML instead of through t(). Examples: Todo.tsx:643 'Plan with AI ✦', Todo.tsx:324 'View on Google Maps →', Todo.tsx:179/204 `Open ${p.name} on Google Maps`, Todo.tsx:241 'Hide details'/'Show details', todoMarkers.ts:157 'On your to-do list' pill + :145 'Day ${n}' chip + :151 'View on Google Maps →', TodoListPanel.tsx:373-374 Maps title/aria, dayDetailModal.ts:611 `${remaining} of ${items.length} left` (the initial render at :472 uses t('dayDetail.checklistRemaining') but the toggle handler overwrites it with the English literal).
- **Repro:** Switch the app to Spanish/French/Portuguese, open /todo and a to-do place's map InfoWindow: 'Plan with AI', 'View on Google Maps', 'On your to-do list', 'Day 2', and the Maps tooltips render in English; toggle a checklist item in a day modal and the summary flips to '2 of 5 left'.
- **Suggested fix:** Route each of these through t() with new/existing keys across en/es/fr/pt (reuse todo._/dayDetail._ namespaces; the day-checklist toggle should re-use t('dayDetail.checklistRemaining', { remaining, total }) instead of the English template literal).

### DSGN-090 — [P3][i18n] 'Day deleted' success toast is a hardcoded English string (i18n gap)

_trips · verdict: **confirmed** · confidence 0.90_

- **Files:** `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home/handlers.ts:321`, `frontend/static/js/src/pages/home-mount/handlers.ts:321`
- **Symptom:** After deleting an itinerary day, a Spanish/French/Portuguese user sees the toast 'Day deleted' in English, breaking the otherwise-localized UI.
- **Root cause:** deleteDay’s onConfirm calls showLiquidAlert('Day deleted') with a literal string instead of t(...) (home-mount/handlers.ts:321). Every other toast in this flow uses t(); this one was missed. The confirm dialog itself (errors.deleteDayTitle/Body/ConfirmBtn) is correctly localized, so only the success toast is wrong.
- **Repro:** 1. Switch app language to Español/Français/Português. 2. Delete a numbered day. 3. The success toast reads 'Day deleted' in English.
- **Suggested fix:** Add a localized key (e.g. errors.dayDeletedToast / toasts.dayDeleted) to en/es/fr/pt and replace the literal with t('...').
- **Verifier:** Confirmed showLiquidAlert('Day deleted') literal at home-mount/handlers.ts:321 (grep shows it is the sole occurrence), surrounded by t()-localized strings; note the finding's other cited path pages/home/handlers.ts does not exist, but the real file home-mount/handlers.ts has exactly the cited i18n gap, so P3.
